Impending Renewal of Warfare in Guangxi Province 97

Long Yun's Troops Advance Towards Baise

Guangdong Authorities Dispatch Troops to Guard Against Communists

Guangzhou Correspondence: The situation regarding the war in Guangxi Province has remained unchanged in recent days, allowing Chen Jitang, the Eighth Route Army Commander-in-Chief, to return to Guangdong at his leisure. It is reported that the Sixth and Eighth Route Armies stationed between Wan and Gui continue to monitor the movements of the enemy across the river, preparing equipment for crossing. They await the arrival of Guizhou and Yunnan troops into Guangxi before launching a full-scale encirclement of Xun and Liu. Recent reports indicate that a contingent of Guizhou troops has reached Guangxi's western border. Long Yun of Yunnan Province has recently intensified mobilization efforts. The Sixth Route Army Headquarters sent representative He Zifang to Yunnan to coordinate military action against Guangxi. In his recent letter from Yunnan, He stated that he had been personally instructed by Yigong (Zhu Shaoliang's alias) in Wuzhou to discuss the troop deployment with Chairman Long upon his return to Yunnan, which was deeply appreciated. Specifically, the three divisions of Lu (Han), Zhu (Xu), and Zhang (Fengchun) have been ordered to depart by the end of the month. He anticipates returning to Wuzhou to report on the troop movements immediately after their departure. Local authorities have recently received a crucial telegram from Yunnan Province stating that Long Yun, following central orders, has mobilized eighteen regiments to enter Guangxi's borders, awaiting orders. On the 26th of last month, a mobilization rally was held, where various sectors of Yunnan society convened to bid farewell to the Tenth Route Army's campaign against the rebels. Long delivered an impassioned speech at the rally, emphasizing the revolutionary soldier's duty to uphold the central government, solidify the party and nation, and sacrifice all. The entire venue erupted in thunderous applause. The shipment of the eighteen regiments is expected to be completed this week, reaching Yan Yin and other locations. Based on the above telegrams, a large-scale war in Guangxi is expected soon. In Guangdong Province, the border defense along the southern route and the West River is quite solid. However, the situation along the northeastern border has become slightly unsettled recently. After fleeing from Nanxiong back to southern Jiangxi, the Zhu-Peng communist bandits exploited the weakness of the Jiangxi border defense, engaging in disruptive activities. Furthermore, the defection of Jin Handing's troops further deteriorated security in southeastern Jiangxi. Rumors suggest that the two brigade commanders of Jin's division, Wei Chu and Zhou Zhiqun, were former subordinates of Yang Ximin of the Yunnan army. There are concerns that Yang may be communicating with military leaders in the north, implying Yang's involvement in Jin's defection. Reportedly, the defected troops have infiltrated eastern Jiangxi, seemingly planning to pass through Ruijin, Huichang, and Xunwu counties before retreating into Guangdong's borders. To prevent communist incursion, Guangdong authorities have dispatched a portion of the 61st Division from Chaozhou-Meizhou, along with Zhang Zhen's Fujian troops who recently arrived, to deploy along the Jiangxi-Guangdong border. To bolster forces in the East River region, the Eighth Route Army Headquarters sent a team on the Xin Chang steamship to Shantou on the 26th of last month, which disembarked entirely on the morning of the 28th. They immediately boarded the fifth Chaozhou-Shantou train to Chaoan, deploying to various locations along the upper reaches of the Han River. The Zhu-Peng communist bandits have been quite rampant in Nankang, Daping, Xinfeng, Anyuan, Dingnan, Longnan, Xunwu, Huichang and other places in southern Jiangxi recently. Zhu De's contingent in Xinfeng also seems to be eyeing Nanxiong. Fearing insufficient defense forces, various groups in Nanxiong telegraphed the provincial authorities yesterday, requesting assistance. Military authorities are dispatching additional troops for suppression today the 30th on twenty Guangdong railway cars, expected to arrive in Nanxiong tomorrow. (May 2nd)

Vigorous Relief Efforts for Rice Shortage in Anhui's Capital 98

One Approach is Lending Grain from the Ten Thousand Trillion Granary

Another Approach is Allocating Military Rice from Headquarters

The rice shortage in Anhui's capital has intensified recently. Despite various attempts to provide relief, it has not been alleviated. Previously, the Civil Food Maintenance Association allocated 800 shi of intercepted rice to various rice shops for sale, which has been gradually sold. However, as the provincial government observed that the source of rice from the surrounding rural areas had almost completely ceased after the rice shortage in the provincial capital, they dispatched personnel to Shanghai to purchase western rice, which was a slow measure to address the situation. They then decided to allocate over 10,000 shi of grain from the Ten Thousand Trillion Granary, originally intended for emergency needs in the provincial capital. Responding to requests from numerous agencies and organizations to borrow grain for relief, a temporary discussion meeting was convened on the 30th of last month to discuss solutions. The Department of Civil Affairs proposed drafting a plan to mill and sell rice from the Ten Thousand Trillion Granary, which was approved. The plan included: (1) The provincial government would entrust the United Charitable Organizations with the milling and sale of rice from the Ten Thousand Trillion Granary. (2) The price of the rice would be set at ten yuan per shi. (3) The amount of rice sold to each person would be limited to three sheng per day. (4) The United Charitable Organizations would devise the sales method and submit it to the provincial government for approval. (5) The Anqing Civil Food Maintenance Committee would be responsible for unclogging the rice supply and suppressing hoarding. The Civil Food Maintenance Association has followed these guidelines. The provincial government, noting that 2,800 shi of military rice procured by headquarters remained in Gaohebu, yet to be shipped out, planned to temporarily borrow it for immediate relief, with the intention of returning it once the Shanghai rice shipment arrived. They immediately telegraphed Secretary-General Shao in Hankou, requesting that Commander-in-Chief Jiang be notified. They subsequently received a reply from Shao stating that the Commander-in-Chief had approved the allocation, instructing them to contact the station. They promptly telegraphed the station headquarters, requesting the rice procurement committee to comply, to which they agreed. With these measures, the rice shortage issue may find some resolution. (May 3rd)

Quick News from Wuhu 99

The educational funding for Anhui Province was explicitly stipulated by the Ministry of Finance and the University Council, that ten million yuan should be preferentially allocated from the central tax revenues remitted by Anhui Province, to maintain education. However, only 30% of the educational funds for March of the 19th year have been received recently, resulting in arrears of two hundred thousand yuan. The Anhui Provincial Educators' Association believes that the livelihoods of educators cannot be sustained, and this continued delay is dangerous. In addition to demanding funds from the provincial government, they dispatched representatives Wang Dianping, Cheng You, and Dong Zhuqun to Wuhu to collaborate with the Wuhu Educators' Association in urging the Anhui Finance Commissioner's Office of the Ministry of Finance to release the funds. If a solution cannot be found, they will go to Beijing to petition both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Education.

Over a thousand bandits from Guangde County were previously suppressed by the Third Battalion dispatched by the Weishutuan (Garrison Regiment) under Lü Xueshu. The captured bandit leader, Yang Shikait, has been executed on the spot by order of Garrison Regiment Leader Lü. Troops were dispatched to pursue the remaining bandits who fled to Changxing, on the border between Zhejiang and Anhui.

Various groups convened a meeting this morning at the Ge Wu stage to commemorate the May Fifth National Humiliation Day. Over three hundred representatives attended. Government agencies and shops were closed for the day.

The Supervisory Committee of the Municipal Party Headquarters has requested the Provincial Party Headquarters to dismiss and punish Li Gengchang, the Wuhu Customs Superintendent, for allowing the export of rice, causing panic in the food supply and arousing public anger. At one o'clock this afternoon, a band of over twenty bandits suddenly appeared near the Guangfu Islet area of Yiji Mountain in Wuhu, attempting to rob. The local self-defense corps immediately mobilized to encircle and capture them. The bandits opened fire. The General Headquarters of the Public Security Brigade, the Garrison Regiment Headquarters, and the Public Security Bureau dispatched troops to assist in the joint attack. After an hour of intense fighting, the self-defense corps killed four bandits on the spot. The rest fled in a northwest direction. The Garrison Regiment has dispatched troops to pursue them. Huang Bao Ying, the leader of the Self-Defense Corps, was also wounded by the bandits. (May 5th)

New Situation in Fujian's Party and Political Affairs 100

The New Provincial Steering Committee is About to be Established

Chen Peikun Temporarily Assumes the Position of Provincial Chairman

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Party Affairs Steering Committee originally consisted of nine members. Following the January 6th coup this year, Ding Chao Wu and Yang Shuzhuang went to Shanghai, Fang Zhi and Feng Siding went to Beijing, Lin Xueyuan returned to Zhangzhou, Lin Jihua resigned, and Chen Naiyuan was arrested. Only Zhan Diaoyuan and Feng Ji'an remained in the province. Recently, Zhan Diaoyuan requested leave to return to his hometown to rescue his entire family, who were captured by communists in Longyan. Feng Ji'an is being treated for lung disease at the Chaijing Hospital. As a result, the Party Headquarters is without leadership. The county Party Headquarters in southern and western Fujian, due to their different positions from the provincial authorities, established a United Association of Thirty-Two County Party Headquarters, sending representatives to Beijing to request the reorganization of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and expressing their intention to temporarily suspend acceptance of provincial orders pending reorganization. Therefore, the Fujian Provincial Party Affairs, along with politics, have been effectively stalled since the beginning of this year. In order to strengthen the organization of the Fujian Provincial Party, the Central Committee decided at its standing meeting on April 24th to recall all nine current Fujian Provincial Party Affairs Steering Committee members and appoint Zhan Diaoyuan, Feng Ji'an, Kang Shaozhou, Chen Lianfang, and Gan Yun as new Steering Committee members. Among these five, Zhan and Feng are continuing from the previous term, Kang and Chen graduated from the Central Party School and currently serve as the Party Affairs Steering Committee members in Siming County, and Gan is a graduate of the Whampoa Military Academy and currently serves as a clerk in the Central Party Headquarters. It is expected that the New Provincial Steering Committee will be established as early as mid-May or as late as late May. Since the coup, the Provincial Government has been jointly maintained by Chairman Yang Shuzhuang and Commissioners Chen Peikun, Jiang Pingfan, and Lin Jinan. The Provincial Affairs Conference has been completely suspended. Subsequently, the three commissioners, Chen, Jiang, and Lin, believing that Yang's prolonged stay in Shanghai made it difficult for him to bear the heavy responsibility, telegraphed their resignations and urged Yang to return quickly. Yang sent Jiang Zhizhuang back to Fujian to comfort and retain the commissioners, and the commissioners temporarily withdrew their resignations. Recently, the National Government sent a telegram from the Civil Service Office to the Provincial Government, stating that, upon the Chairman's instruction, Chen Peikun was appointed to temporarily represent the Chairman's duties until Yang Shuzhuang's return to Fujian. After receiving the telegram, Chen, considering the extremely thorny military and financial affairs in Fujian Province, was unwilling to shoulder this heavy responsibility and telegraphed the National Government to resign. However, as the political affairs in Fujian Province have been stalled for a long time, and the approaching Abolition Calendar Festival coincided with the tense military situation in western Fujian's campaign against the communists, it was necessary to have someone in charge. Despite Chen's firm intention to resign, it is unlikely that the National Government will approve it.

Furthermore, the entire staff of the Department of Civil Affairs suddenly submitted their resignations to the Provincial Government yesterday, the 30th. The resignation letter is as follows: "Submitting a request for resignation: On the morning of the 30th of this month, Zhang Bao Rong, Ke Zhenfu, Wu Huaibing, Shi Jingheng, Zhan Shiting, Zhang Lianli and others, claiming to be representatives of the Army Fourth School's Fujian alumni in the opposition, came to the Department to interfere with the Department's deliberation on the Qingxiang office case of Minyongqing County. Secretary Huang Zuhan received them, but Zhang Bao Rong and others, unable to achieve their unreasonable demands, shouted, made a scene, acted disorderly, and insulted him, and falsely accused the entire Department staff to the government. With the government's credibility swept away in such a manner, it is truly impossible to maintain. We have no choice but to express our feelings and the entire staff presents this request for resignation, humbly requesting your approval." The Fujian Provincial Government is truly beset with troubles. (May 1st)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 101

Change of Command for the Provincial River Police: The headquarters of the first team of the first district of the Jiangsu Provincial River Police, stationed in Songcheng, recently saw the departure of Director of the Minxing District Chi Yaozong. The provincial government appointed Chen to replace him. He Yalin, head of the first team stationed in Songjiang, also received orders from above, and Zhu Chen was appointed as his successor. Zhu arrived in Songjiang on the 5th to take office. Zhu is currently the head of the deputy officer's division of the Songhu Garrison Command, transferred to this position.

Reconstruction of Xiu Bridge and Inspection of Main Roads: Most of the tall bridges on the main roads of this city have been dismantled and rebuilt. The Xiuye Bridge in the western suburbs, rebuilt into a cement and steel reinforced bridge last winter, has been completed. The contractor applied for inspection. The county government appointed staff member Qian Tiansheng, along with district chief Zhong Taichi and Wu, an engineer from the Construction Bureau, to inspect the project. The engineering work was generally satisfactory. Furthermore, residents near the Xiunan and Xitang tall bridges on the opposite bank felt inconvenienced by the lack of easy access. They requested the First District Office to plan the reconstruction and add two level bridges at the eastern and western ferry crossings to alleviate the inconvenience. Although the construction costs are substantial, local residents have expressed their willingness to contribute financially. A meeting will be convened at the Public No. 9 School on the afternoon of the 11th of this month to discuss the implementation plan. Construction is expected to begin once a plan is agreed upon. The reconstruction plan for the Mingxing Bridge in the eastern suburbs is ready and the commencement of construction is near.

Kunshan 102

Tea House Collapse Injures People: The Hong Yun Lou tea house on Gongjian Street in the city, founded by Shandong natives Mr. Li and Mr. Pan, celebrated its opening on the 4th, inviting the Suzhou Xiaotangming opera troupe to perform. The tea house was packed with customers and spectators. At 7:00 PM, the building suddenly collapsed under the weight, injuring over twenty spectators and tea drinkers. Among them, a son of the Wei family was seriously injured and was immediately transported to the Guangren and Kunshan hospitals for treatment. Zou Wuzhi, the director of the Public Security Bureau, dispatched police officers to investigate.

Suzhou 103

Calamity Caused by Horse Riding: Lawsuit Opens in Court: Hong Zhang, a student from Shanghai Minli High School, caused a calamity while riding a horse in Suzhou in March, injuring an old man, Zhou Huchen, who died as a result. After investigation by the Wu County District Court, Zheng was ordered to compensate Zhou's family with 750 yuan for medical expenses and 50 yuan for medical treatment, and sentenced to 50 days of detention with a two-year suspended sentence. Subsequently, the prosecutor appealed the verdict. Zheng hired lawyer Xia Dingrui to defend him in court. The First Criminal Tribunal of the High Court opened the trial yesterday afternoon (the 6th).

Quarry Accident at Jinshan Nanbang Injures People: Villagers near Jinshan Nanbang, outside Xumen, primarily engage in quarrying, transporting and selling stones to various regions. The annual transactions reach tens of thousands of yuan. On the afternoon of the 5th, a client, Ni Yunquan (31 years old, from Jinshanbang), led a group of stonemasons to a nearby mountain to quarry. After using explosives to blast the rocks, they saw a giant rock on top about to fall. They used bricks to prop it up. Upon hearing a cracking sound, they knew the situation was dire and tried to escape, but it was too late. Ni and his partner, Mu Lan (24 years old, from Caoxiang), were crushed to death. After the accident, only a foot of Ni's body remained, the rest was pulverized. Mu Xiulang's body was also a bloody mess, too gruesome to look at. Another worker, Zhou Genyun (22 years old, from Jinshanbang), only injured his right foot and is not in life-threatening danger.

Fengxian 104

Negotiations to Reclaim Rooms Lent to Salt Police: The rooms of the local Xiyisuo (Vocational Training Center) were borrowed by former police chief Li Tianmin from the Qian Industrial Bureau in March of the 16th year of the Republic, as a temporary measure due to his local status. No rent was charged. The lease agreement stipulated that the rooms could be vacated if needed. These rooms have now been designated for use as granaries. Repeated requests for their return have been unsuccessful. The Yicang (Charity Granary) Management Committee, due to the imminent opening of the granaries, could no longer delay, and directly consulted the Songyun Deputy Envoy, who approved the reclamation. However, the Salt Police Bureau has now demanded over five hundred yuan in compensation for repair costs. Former police chief Li, who originally handled the lease, has revealed that the repair costs were fully covered by funds allocated by the Yunfu Envoy and have already been reported, with no further relation. Therefore, the committee has replied based on this information.

New County Chief Imminent: The newly appointed acting county chief of this county, Shen Qingchen, a native of Wujin, is confirmed to arrive to take office on the 13th of this month.

Qingpu 105

Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad: Kidnappers Gu Ahu, Dai Gensen, Zhang Asan, Zhang Genfa, Shen Guilin, and others successively kidnapped Shen Yangxian, Yang Qiusheng of Xiping Township, and Cai Zhaoye of Chen Guoshe Village on August 21st of last year. They also kidnapped Shen Yangxian's grandson, Shen Zhiping, and granddaughter, Shen Meiying. They were arrested by the Provincial Public Security Team, investigated, and processed in the county. The county government interrogated them and, based on the confirmation by the victims in court, determined that Shen Guilin was innocent and allowed bail. Zhang Asan and Zhang Genfa were deemed to have committed less severe crimes and were sentenced separately. Gu Ahu and Dai Gensen were sentenced to death and the provincial government approved the execution. On the morning of May 5th, the two were taken to the execution ground outside the Great West Gate and executed by firing squad.

Five Families in Chai Tang Village Robbed: In Chai Tang Village, near the Bai He Jiang Township in Qingpu, over ten bandits suddenly appeared at around 7:00 PM last night, armed with firearms, and robbed five families, including the Ma family. The Bai He Jiang Self-Defense Corps, upon hearing the alarm, dispatched troops to pursue them, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Wuxi 106

Construction Director Inspects the Xicheng Road: Sun Hongzhe, the director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, accompanied by Yu Tongfu, the chief engineer of the Provincial Highway Bureau, and Gao Chengzhang, the inspector and director of the Savings Preparatory Office, arrived in Wuxi from the province on the 9:10 PM express train. The next morning, they secretly inspected the southern section of the Xicheng Road. In the afternoon, they visited the County Construction Bureau to inquire about everything. Yao Dixing, the director of the Construction Bureau, accompanied them to tour the scenic spots of Meiyuan and Turtle Head Isle and visit the Shen Xin Three Factory. They returned to the city at 6:00 PM and took the train back to the province.

Jailbreak Case Being Tried in Suzhou: On the night of March 26th, a group of seven inmates, including Li Chengguo, a major criminal whose execution had been approved, and Zhang Aqi, escaped from the Wuxi Detention Substation by scaling the wall. Subsequently, Liu Yinqiu, the clerk of the substation, and Jiang Hailin, one of the guards, were arrested. Furthermore, because the inmates used four bellybands to scale the wall, Meng Genyu, the former warden and current warden of Yangzhong, should not have provided the bellybands. Suspecting other circumstances, Meng was brought back from Yangzhong and jointly interrogated by the county at the Wu County District Court. After two interrogations by the Wu District Court, Meng Genyu claimed that the four bellybands were given to the inmates because Zhang Aqi and others needed to do heavy work such as washing rice and carrying water, and it was customary practice in prisons across counties. The Wu District Court deemed Meng innocent and ordered his release on bail. The remaining clerk, Liu Yinqiu, and the guard, Jiang Hailin, were put in shackles and imprisoned.

Request to Revoke Illegal Union: The local Grain and Load Carrying Union recently requested the registration of Chen Fengquan, Gu Jin'an, and others as sub-union, stealing members, changing names, and adding them for the sake of numbers. They requested the county's Reorganization Committee and the County Government to issue an order to the Labour Organization to revoke the registration, to maintain the workers movement. After receiving the report, County Chief Sun of the County's Reorganization Committee instructed the Labor Organization to investigate and handle the matter.

Police Shoot Suspected Bandit: Ding Genda of Jing Ting Xia, near Outang Bridge in the Fourth District of Wuxi County, had been suspected of being a bandit in Shanghai. He returned home from Shanghai, and the police from the Ninth Branch of the Public Security Bureau of the district were notified and dispatched to arrest him on the night of the 5th. The suspect tried to escape by climbing onto the roof. The police opened fire and killed Ding on the spot. Lu, the chief of the branch, has reported the incident to the County Public Security Bureau for verification.

He arrived in Chencheng from Suzhou by early ship on the 4th. He met with former county head Shen and Chief of Public Security Bureau Zhang to briefly discuss the Hong Wan case. Outgoing county head Shen Bingyan and bureau chief Zhang Pinquan still need to go to the province. Numerous Robbery Cases in Beiwai: A robbery case occurred in the past evening (the 4th). Shensen Taijia in Qixu Li, Beiwai Wu Baodun Mengjili Chengan Temple, was about to marry off his daughter, and the wedding gifts and clothes were robbed.

Nantong 108

Arrest of Bandit Leaders from Nantong and Rugao: Bandits were rampant at the junction of Nantong and Rugao counties. The bandit leader, Tang Jianquan, sneaked into the Pingchao district. The district office arrested the culprit. The culprit committed the most crimes in Rugao. He was escorted to Rugao for trial.

Qidong Labour Unrest Settled: A strike suddenly broke out at the Dasheng Second Cotton Mill in Jiulongzhen, Qidong at the end of last month. The Hu Battalion of the Fifth Division stationed in Tongzhou rushed to suppress the rebellion. In cooperation with the county police force, they cracked down on communist institutions near the factory, killing seven bandits and arresting sixty-one. The labour unrest has been resolved. Hu Battalion has returned to Nantong.

Measures to Suppress Bandits and Communists: Bandits and communists in the eastern and western countryside of Nantong colluded, calling themselves the Red Army, causing great disturbances. The representatives of the military, police, party and government agencies have decided to thoroughly suppress them within a month, that is, the Hu Battalion of the Fifth Division will join forces with the provincial and county police forces to advance to the bandit areas. The public security bureaus and police forces of various districts and the guard regiments will continue to clear the countryside. At the same time, the county party department and the county government will stipulate measures for reporting bandits and communists and announce their implementation. Those who are forced to become bandits are allowed to surrender and be exempted from prosecution.

Prisoner Food Problem at Detention Center: The detention center in this county has no money for prisoner food, and the county government is losing money, because the number of detainees has recently increased to more than 300. Asking the province to approve the actual expenditures, the approval was given to the finance department for review.

Bandit Police in Sanyu Reclamation Area: A large number of bandits are gathered in Sanyu Reclamation Area. The garrisoned special police team requested the county for emergency help. County Chief Zhang sent the county police team to suppress the bandits.

Funing 110

Construction Bureau Section Chief Arrested for Smoking Opium: Chen Jingyu, the section chief of the Construction Bureau, was smoking opium in the bureau yesterday. Xiang Lianqiu, a member of the Drug Resistance Society, found out about it and led a group of society members, along with Lu Zhonghao, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, to the bureau. They found Section Chief Chen was on the bed in a haze. He was arrested along with multiple pieces of smoking equipment and sent to the county government. The court opened the trial and sentenced him to a fine of 300 yuan and four months in prison. It is said that Lu Yaochang, the director of the bureau, resigned due to the disgrace.

Jiaxing 111

Continued Report on the Chengxi Fish Farming Dispute: It was previously reported that a native of Shaoxing who lives in Youchegang, Jiaxing, had a fight with villagers in Yang'an Town over fish farming. It has now been learned that a Shaoxing native, Yan, and others raised a large sum of money and formed the Taishan Fish Farming Site, setting up barriers without official permission. The nearby Yang'an town villagers removed the barriers. After receiving the news, the Shaoxing natives gathered a large number of people, armed with oars, and hired the seventh and eighth patrol boats of the water police. They dragged them ashore in Yang'an town with a coal ship, beat Zhou Fengshan, the son of the village chief. Angering the villagers, they rang the gongs to gather a crowd. Knowing that they were about to be overwhelmed, they escaped on the boats. Shen Lianqing and Shen Wuer, natives of Shaoxing, were unable to escape. They were tied up by the villagers and the two boats and two sharp knives were seized. After the villagers took revenge, they beat the two men who had been captured.

Near News:嘉兴因民食奇昂,经县政府召集各法团代表,组织平糶委员会,业已推定常务筹议进行.

Organizing Fair Price:

Recent news: Jiaxing is in the midst of a food shortage. The county government convened the representatives of each legal group to organize the Fair Price Committee.

We learned of its method.

(一) Set the use of funds to 15,000 yuan, except for all the reserve fair-price donations of silver, 4643.338 yuan under the 16-year compensation fund, other funds will be borrowed from the county.

(二)The Rice Industry Association in the city will ask the merchants in all areas to purchase a total of 7500 stone small cross Ocean rice for future use.

(三) Agreed on poor household standards, divide each of the village meeting to investigate, and then distribute the amount of fair rice in the quantity after sampling (四)Fair price is determined by the Rice Bank's price, each stone will be sold for 2 Yuan less.

Jiashan 112

Villagers of Xu Five District Robbed at Residence: Fu Erguan's home, a villager in the Xu Five District outside Nanmen, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits armed with rapid-firing guns around 11 PM on the third day. They broke into the house and looted clothing and ornaments worth over 100 yuan.

Abolishment of Land Reporting Office: Chen Rangqing, the director of the Land Reporting Office, was ordered by the county magistrate to abolish the office immediately. It was closed at the end of April. All matters relating to Chen Gen (land registration) handled by village and neighborhood meeting halls were transferred to the county government, and Autonomous Instructors such as Li Bingcong were instructed to strictly urge completion of the report.

Zhang Yousong of Dayun Temple Kidnapped: It is reported that Zhang Yousong of Dayun Temple in this county was kidnapped from his home on the night of March 30th. Eight days later, arsonists set fire to a boat and left a letter, suggesting a location for negotiation in a remote area, but no one went. On the sixteenth, another letter arrived, again suggesting a meeting time. Although someone was entrusted to negotiate, the asking price was too high and no agreement was reached. Another meeting time was arranged, but due to the remote location, no one dared to go. Half a month has passed with no news. His family and relatives are anxiously consulting oracles daily. It was heard yesterday that a relative, Mr. Yi, went to Shanghai to inquire about the situation, but it is unknown if there is any progress.

Ningbo 113

Soldiers Selling Private Salt: Yesterday morning, when the Zhenhai steamship arrived at port, over twenty soldiers were found carrying multiple packages of private salt. They were seized by salt police, and three soldiers, Dong Guodong, Jiang Shengxiong, and Yang Bin, were arrested. They confessed to being soldiers from the Zhenhai Suiyuan Artillery Battery. The Salt Bureau, unsure if they were imposters since the soldiers were in uniform but not wearing insignia, inquired with the Artillery Headquarters. The Chief of Staff, Mr. Chen, dispatched Zhang Jiaxiang to Ningbo, who took Dong Guodong and the other two soldiers back to Zhenhai to be severely punished according to the law.

News of Yin County Magistrate Being Transferred to Jiaxing: Chen Baolin, the magistrate of Yin County, has been in office for over a year. According to news from the provincial authorities, the Civil Affairs Department has decided to transfer Chen Baolin to be the magistrate of Jiaxing County. Wu Changchun, the current magistrate of Dinghai County, will fill the vacancy in Yin County.

Yang Zhonglu's Young Son Kidnapped: More than ten bandits, armed with guns, suddenly arrived at the home of merchant Yang Zhonglu in Shijing Village, Lianshan District, Fenghua, and kidnapped his seven-year-old son. The local defense corps is searching in all directions, but there is no trace of the bandits.

Thunderstorm Kills Three: Yesterday at 9:00 AM, a violent storm with thunder and lightning struck both sides of the river. Xu Liangsheng’s small boat, carrying Chen Xinfu, a farmer from Yao Nan Ao Jia Bu, his wife, and their four children, was caught in the storm. While passing the Jiangbei Fushi Pavilion on the river, the boat was overturned by the wind. The boat owner Xu Liangsheng and Chen's wife were rescued, but Chen Xinfu and one of his children drowned. It is reported that Chen’s seventeen-year-old daughter came to Ningbo to buy her wedding trousseau in preparation for her wedding next month, but tragically met with this disaster. At the same time, a barge unloading rice from the Longshan ship in Xiabaisha River was also sunk by the wind and waves, resulting in the loss of forty bags of rice.

Shaoxing 114

Fundraising Methods for the Defense Corps: The funds for the Shaoxing Defense Corps have already used 20,000 yuan from the county treasury by April. The Defense Committee held a full meeting on the afternoon of the 4th to find ways to maintain operations. It was decided to first raise 50,000 yuan, allocating the amount according to the initial setup cost rule, multiplied by five.

Hangzhou 115

Silk Cocoon Merchants Seek Relief: Silk merchants in Zhejiang province are seeking relief due to the Japanese government's allocation of over ten million yuan to support its silk merchants, instructing them not to sell at low prices, resulting in low international market transaction volumes. Zhejiang silk has been affected and cannot be sold. Cocoon businesses that have not yet leased locations are without prospects, and those who have leased are retreating, resulting in significant losses. After discussion, various guilds have submitted petitions to the provincial government, requesting assistance.

Yang Shuzhuang Comes to Hangzhou to Recuperate: Naval Minister Yang Shuzhuang went from Mogan Mountain to Shanghai and then to Beijing on official business. According to news from the transportation sector yesterday, Yang has finished his affairs in Beijing and will return to Shanghai to have his health examined by doctors. He will then return to Hangzhou to recuperate, but it has not yet been decided whether he will stay at West Lake or Mogan Mountain.

New Statistics on Relief Efforts: According to the latest statistics on relief efforts in Zhejiang province, there are a total of 355 relief organizations in the two cities and 70 counties of the province. In the past two years, approximately 62,294 people have been rescued.

Abolishing the Tax Collection Contractor System: The Zhejiang Department of Finance is proceeding with the abolition of the tax collection contractor system. Besides having already transferred the foreign cloth tax in six districts, the provincial sugar tax, and the Hangzhou-Shaoxing artificial silk tax to be managed by specialized bureaus established by the province, preparations are currently underway for other taxes, such as the Guancheng Hall [opium] tax, the Huashe Huawei Daidui [unclear, possibly local taxes] tax, and the Ningbo grass mat tax. Officials were dispatched yesterday to investigate the actual situation regarding the Hangzhou-Shaoxing gold, ginseng, and bird's nest tax, the Jinhua Daidui tax, and the Ningbo grass mat tax to make informed decisions.

Price Increase for Grain Relief: The Zhejiang province borrowed 300,000 yuan to manage grain price stabilization. The original price for grain allocated to each county was 12.6 yuan per stone, but it has been raised to 13.6 yuan since yesterday. It is said that this is because the purchase price has increased, and this increase is unavoidable. The 13.6 yuan does not include shipping costs.

Wuyuan 116

Bandits Led by Fang Disrupt Leping: Since Fang Zhimin established a base in Gandon, local areas have suffered immensely. Although provincial troops have repeatedly attempted to suppress them, the bandits are scattered and difficult to eliminate. In recent months, Guangxin and Dexing Wannian counties have been harassed by bandits. Around the 20th of this month, a large group of bandits led by Fang entered Mingshan, fifteen li outside the city of Leping. Mingshan is located in the coal mining area of ​​the Po Le Coal Mining Company, because the bandits were coveting the Company's police guns, they searched the mountains and could not find anything. They then arrested two company officials and looted 7,000 yuan. Fortunately, the Yue Huang Regiment stationed in Leping, upon hearing the alarm, led a team to Mingshan to pursue the bandits, who were no match for the regiment and fled. According to various reports, the bandits are still planning to gather forces for a large-scale attack on the city. People are increasingly panicked, and all shops have closed. The whole city has stepped up security. On the 26th, a Communist bandit was escorted from Wannian. He was the elder brother of bandit leader Shao Shiping, and had been sent to various places to promote Communism. He was arrested after his plot was exposed. He was beheaded at 1:00 PM that afternoon after being interrogated by the regimental headquarters. Security is still very tight today to prevent unforeseen events. Police are being sent to search for remaining party members. It is reported that the tea market in Hekou and Dexing is difficult to open due to rampant banditry. Tea merchants in Hekou are advising each other not to enter the mountains due to the presence of many bandits. Although new tea from Qimen is being picked and processed, the tea market has been greatly affected because all the merchants are stopping business and has been affected greatly.

Letter

Letter from Wu Jinming, Chief of Fengjing Public Security Bureau 117

Dear Sirs, I recently read in your newspaper on the 5th of this month in the Jia Shan news column that "Dai Fengjing Branch Chief arbitrarily dismissed the patrol leader, causing public indignation." This is not in accordance with the facts. The Yaozhuang Bridge Outpost is under the direct control of the Fengjing Branch. The patrol leader's competence is the responsibility of the Fengjing Branch Chief. This patrol leader, Cao Peng, has acted improperly since taking office. Using the county bureau as a shield, he has repeatedly defied orders from the Fengjing Branch Chief. For instance, when the Xu Daxiong (Tai Bao Ashu) bandit group came to Yaozhuang Bridge for the third time, kidnapping Yang Xiaodi’s daughter again, the patrol leader did not report it to the Branch Chief. Also, he collaborated with the Yao West Village Defense Corps to capture the bandit hideout Li Rong's aunt and seized a lot of stolen goods without notifying the Branch Chief. He instead reported directly to the County Bureau, ignoring the Branch Chief. He was ordered to investigate, but only mentioned the surname Li in the report, not the name. He repeatedly ignored warnings. A telegram was sent to County Magistrate Shen to inform Bureau Chief Gu to take action, but the County Bureau Chief protected his person, and did nothing. The Branch Chief believed that he was deliberately obstructing and becoming too big to control, so he ordered his dismissal and put him under supervision, replacing him with first-class policeman Liu Zurong as acting patrol leader, and it has already been reported to the county government. However, this patrol leader, Cao Peng, feared punishment and fled, making a false report to Bureau Chief Gu. On the 1st and 2nd of this month, he dispatched forty armed policemen, and illegally arrested third-class policeman Chen Fude and acting patrol leader Liu Zurong. On May 1st, Branch Chief went to Shanghai on official business to investigate kidnappings and requested a three-day leave. Upon returning to the bureau, he reported to County Magistrate Shen, who also expressed dissatisfaction and released and reinstated the arrested Liu as the acting patrol leader, sending Secretary Hu to instruct Bureau Chief Gu to deal with the one-sided story, in order to obscure the truth. Your newspaper upholds justice, so I am listing the facts and requesting a correction. Sincerely yours, Wu Jinming, Fengjing Branch Chief, Jia Shan County Government Public Security Bureau, May 5th.

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education 118

Investigating the Social Education Situation in Provinces and Cities

Report Submission Deadline: End of May

In order to investigate the state of social education, the Ministry of Education has compiled national social education statistics. It previously issued forms, ordering education departments of various provinces and education bureaus of special municipalities to fill them out and submit them. In order to complete the national social education survey for the seventeenth year and to facilitate the filling and submission process, two types of statistical survey forms for social education in the seventeenth year have been specially designed (divided into Form 1 and Form 2, Form 1 being for surveying all social education facilities outside of schools, and Form 2 being for surveying various supplementary schools and public schools within the scope of social education). Along with the order, the forms will be sent to the provincial education departments and municipal education bureaus, which will be required to fill out the forms immediately upon receipt. They do not need to be forwarded to each county to avoid delays. The various social education endeavors listed in the forms, such as educational undertakings, if the provincial departments or bureaus have not yet organized them, or if the counties have not yet completed the reports, the provincial departments or bureaus may submit those that have been organized and reported first. All must be filled out and submitted to the ministry by the end of May, so that statistics can be reviewed and completed early.

Statistics on Students in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province Over the Years 119

The Number of Enrolled Children Increases Year by Year

Except for a Decrease in the Fifteenth Year

The Jiangsu Provincial United Office for Preparing Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province has submitted various tables, such as statistics on teachers and a general overview of compulsory education, compiled from the results of investigations by various counties in Jiangsu Province for the seventeenth year of the Republic, to the Ministry of Education and distributed them to various counties for reference. The office has now compiled another type of statistical table on the number of elementary school children in Jiangsu Province over the years. The main point is to observe the growth, decline, progress, and regress in the number of children enrolled in compulsory education in various counties from the first year of the Republic to the most recent year, a total of seventeen years. The number of school children in each county and city in Jiangsu Province is listed clearly. This survey and statistics required great effort. The total number of school children (including primary schools and elementary departments of primary schools) in various cities and counties of Jiangsu Province for each year is recorded below:

(1) First year of the Republic: 200,456 people. (2) Second year: 201,567 people. (3) Third year: 229,761. (4) Fourth year: 260,876 people. (5) Fifth year: 284,809 people. (6) Sixth year: 297,697. (7) Seventh year: 322,991 people. (8) Eighth year: 341,930 people. (9) Ninth year: 369,099 people. (10) Tenth year: 399,751 people. (11) Eleventh year: 419,284 people. (12) Twelfth year: 435,775 people. (13) Thirteenth year: 449,510 people. (14) Fourteenth year: 474,426 people. (15) Fifteenth year: 395,922 people. (16) Sixteenth year: 437,979 people. (17) Seventeenth year: 507,644 people.

According to the above statistics, the number of enrolled children increases year by year, except for the fifteenth year, which showed a decrease of 78,504 people compared to the previous year. This was because the revolution first came to Jiangsu in that year, and schools in various counties were inevitably shut down due to the military situation. From the sixteenth year to the seventeenth year, as the period of political tutelage gradually arrived, the number of enrolled children increased dramatically compared to before.

The oppression and aggression our nation has suffered from imperialism is not a matter of a day or two. Looking back, most of the masses are adopting an attitude of not asking and not hearing, which is truly heartbreaking. Sports

Central University Wins Jiangnan University Games Championship 123

Winning Ten of Fifteen Events, Totaling 81.5 Points

Jinan Second with Three Points Less, Jiaotong Third, Guanghua Fourth

Wang Jihuai of Guanghua is Individual Champion with Twenty-Two Points

New Meet Records Set in Four Events, New National Record Set in One Event

The fourth Jiangnan University Athletic Association Games concluded yesterday afternoon around 5:00 PM. Central University won the championship with 81.5 points, while Jinan University was second with only three points less. Jiaotong University was third and Guanghua University was fourth, with only one point separating them. This shows the average strength of the schools and the intensity of the competition.

Good Performance at the Games

Yesterday's weather was sunny and warm, and students from various schools enthusiastically attended the event. The performance in the various sports was not weak. The pole vault was one of the most exciting events. The results of the long-distance races were somewhat affected by the headwind. However, Jinan University's outstanding talent and Zhong Lianji's sprint in the final ten meters were not diminished by the headwind. In the fifteen events over two days, new meet records were set in the hurdles, discus, and 800-meter relay, and a national record was broken in the long jump.

Central University is Well-Rounded

Overall, there was intense competition between Central University and Jinan University in various events. Jinan University excelled in short-distance races, while Central University was superior in field events and long-distance races. Central University also dominated the hurdles, which led to Jinan University being overtaken by three points. Zhao Rugong, Tu Chuan Yao, Zhang Yuansheng, Chen Ling, and Jiang Jingnan performed very well for Central University. The fifteen final events were dominated by them, making them the five heroes of the Central University team.

1. Central University: 81.5 points

3. Jiaotong University: 48 points

4. Guanghua University: 47 points

5. Chinese University: 24 points

6. Daxia University: 6 points

7. Chizhi University: 0 points

A Gathering of Heroes 125

The Chinese Baseball Field

Practice Began Yesterday

Preparing for Three Major Battles

The Achievements of Sixteen Players

The Chinese baseball team of this session is still represented by the overseas Chinese from Honolulu. Yesterday afternoon at three o'clock, they arrived at the Chinese baseball field to begin practicing, preparing for three major battles with the best players from the United States and Japan in Shanghai. It is scheduled to play against the United States on the 8th and 10th, and against Japan on the 11th. Liu Dacheng, a famous Chinese player in Shanghai, also attended the practice yesterday. The team of sixteen representatives consists of veteran players and promising newcomers. Here is a description of their achievements for introduction.

Mr. Zheng Yunyu was the official catcher of the previous baseball team. This time, he came to China with the entire team and was promoted to a key management position, becoming the soul of the team and also serving as one of the catchers. He has been immersed in baseball for ten years.

Mr. Feng Enci is the coach of the entire team, holding a central and crucial position. He is considered the backbone of the Honolulu baseball community. Since joining the baseball world, he has been involved for twenty-three years. Countless young talents have been nurtured by him, and his students can be said to be all over the island. His father had eleven children in total, all of whom loved sports, and Mr. Feng was particularly outstanding. The son of a distinguished family lives up to his name. As a child, he ran fifty yards in five and one-fifth seconds. Although he is now the oldest member of the team, he still moves with agility. This is his first time attending the Far Eastern Games, and he will surely have a good performance.

Photo of the Chinese Baseball Team by Mo Tianxiang

Mr. Cai Yunping is a first-class catcher in Honolulu. In the local commercial baseball competition of the previous session, his team, the Iron Factory Team, was able to win the championship largely due to his efforts. Since then, he has been praised by everyone in the baseball world. Recently, he was elected as one of the representatives, and he is still comfortably serving as a catcher, completely as expected.

Mr. Yu Xian is a catcher and first baseman for the team. He is a promising young player with a very bright future. This is his first time attending.

Lin Yan, the first baseman, is also participating in the conference for the first time. He is skilled in various sports and is a well-rounded athlete.

Mr. Lu Shujie has enjoyed a reputation in the baseball world for the past fifteen years and is one of the most experienced players. This is his first time attending, and he has been elected as the team's vice-captain, which shows his talent.

Mr. He Donghan has strong arms and is good at throwing. In the previous conference, he showed his bravery and added color to the team. He is back again this time, looking even more formidable.

Mr. Feng Yuhe is the sole shortstop in Honolulu. In recent years, no one has surpassed him. This is the second time he has served the Chinese team, and he will surely have a better performance than before.

Mr. Zhang Rongan is the youngest member of the entire team, agile and unmatched. He throws and catches with his left hand with ease. The left field position is his strength.

Li Li is one of the many players in the team who are good at throwing. During the previous conference, his talent was highly valued by the Japanese and Filipinos. This is his second time attending, and his skills have greatly improved. He serves as a right fielder and third baseman.

Mr. Yang Dongzhao's skills were appreciated by people in the previous conference. He is young and eager to improve. He has improved a lot since the last time we met. His second attendance will surely bring an amazing performance. He serves as a right fielder.

Mr. Ye Junxian is a promising newcomer, and his performance skills have been praised by veteran players, so he was also selected as one of the representatives. He is good at using his left hand, so he is suitable for the left field position.

Zhong You is the chief among the four pitchers this time. His pitches are twisting and powerful, making them difficult to catch. The outcome of the conference championship in the future depends on his skills. Due to professional reasons, he was unable to attend the previous conference. This time he is participating, adding a lot of strength. There is hope for the championship.

Mr. Cheng Guanbing is also one of the pitchers, with a quick wrist and good at changing his pitches. This is the second time that Mr. Cheng has served China.

In the previous China-Philippines battle, the Filipinos were unable to cross the Lei River due to Mr. Chen Lanfang's efforts. This time, he is contributing to the Chinese team again and should be even more impressive.

He Yupeng is a promising newcomer among the pitchers. This is his first time attending the conference, but he is already a well-known figure in the Honolulu baseball community.

Overseas Chinese in Kobe 126

Welcome the Honolulu Chinese Baseball Team

The Honolulu Overseas Chinese baseball team has overcome the hardships of travel and returned to participate in the Far Eastern Games to serve the motherland. At around 10:00 AM on May 3rd, they arrived safely in Kobe on the Empress of Canada. Those who greeted them at the pier included representative Hui Yanhua, teachers from the Tongwen School, and the team leader Feng Yinrui, and manager Zheng Yunyu. After a brief conversation, they drove to the Tongwen School for a rest. At 1:00 PM, they responded to the invitation of interested overseas Chinese in Kobe and went to the First Restaurant for a welcoming banquet. Those who attended included Li Shuan, Wen Chaoying, Wang Chongshan, Huang Shikuang, Zheng Boling, Guo Rigen, Zeng Xiju, Zheng Zongqi, Zheng Huimin, Ren Chuanbo, Zheng Sipei, Feng Houhe, He Jinben, Zeng Yanhua, and Zhang Renjun. Representative Wen delivered a welcome speech and encouraged them to strive. Lu Shujie, a representative from Honolulu, stood up to give a thank you speech. In the afternoon at 3:00 PM, they drove to various places in the city for sightseeing. In the late afternoon at 6:00 PM, many overseas Chinese went to say goodbye and made arrangements to meet again.

Chinese Basketball Team 127

Won Against the Fanwangdu Team Again Last Night

Final Score 49 to 21

The Chinese basketball team played against the Fanwangdu team at 7:00 PM last night at the China Basketball Hall. Fanwangdu's defeat was foreseeable even before the game started. However, the team's outstanding performance last night exceeded our expectations. Everyone worked hard and spared no effort. Sullivan, coached by John, and Qu Hongren guarded the backcourt, with strict precautions. Tang Baokun, the forward of the Chinese team, was a brave general, but last night he was closely watched by Sullivan and Qu, taking turns, unable to move. He did not score a single point in the first half. At the end of the second half, due to Fanwangdu's declining strength, Tang was able to take the opportunity to attack and score three goals. This shows the strictness of their defense. In the first half, they competed equally, and the situation was very balanced. The once dominant Chinese team found it difficult to cross the Lei River, and the scores were quite close. The result of the first half was 23 to 13. At the beginning of the second half, Fanwangdu went all out and scored three consecutive goals, and the scores suddenly became very close. The Chinese team then deployed troops and reorganized its forces. A large force entered the championship. Fanwangdu gradually became unsustainable, and coupled with insufficient strength, they fell sharply. Only the Chinese team was seen scoring one goal after another, resulting in a score of 49 to 21. The Chinese team won. The referee was Shu Hong.

Restoring His Reputation Seems Not Far Off

The Japan Sports Association received a telegram from Hong Kong stating that Lin Baohua, our country's tennis representative, has returned to Hong Kong from Saigon due to the approaching conference schedule. Now, he has surpassed Lin in one leap, which is truly alarming to the world. According to Japanese sports experts, our country may not have any hope for this year's tennis championship. Both Break School Records

Fudan University's track and field competition has always been famous and occupies a considerable position in East China. The First Day of the Wuxi Sports Meet 130

31 Schools Participating

Over 4,000 Athletes

A Wuxi dispatch reports that the joint sports meet of public and private primary and secondary schools in the county of Wuxi began yesterday at the public sports field outside the West Gate, lasting for three days. The participating schools included four boys' schools, such as the County Junior Middle School, Private Wuxi Middle School, Furen Middle School, and Kuangcun Middle School, and three girls' schools, such as the County Girls' Middle School and Private Zhongxi Girls' School, and Kuangcun Girls' Middle School. In addition to the County First, Second, Third, Fourth, Fifth, and Sixth Elementary Schools, all registered private elementary schools, such as Tang's Baozi and Yang's, totaling eighteen schools, also participated, making a total of 31 participating public and private boys' and girls' primary and secondary schools. There were as many as 430 individual sports athletes. There were over 4,000 people in group performances. Yesterday, the results of the whole-body exercises, Baduanjin (Shude School), calisthenics (County Fourth School), herd of sheep sticks (Dangkuo Primary School fifth and sixth graders), mass exercises (County Fifth Elementary School fifth and sixth grade boys), and excellent dance (Cai's Elementary School fifth graders) were very good. The 100-meter preliminary rounds were held for four groups of elementary school boys (A, B, C, and D), and the 50-meter preliminary rounds were also held for four groups of elementary school girls (A, B, C, and D).

Local News

Sino-Turkish and Sino-Finnish Commercial Treaties 134

One Will Begin Negotiations

One Will Be Officially Signed

Li Jinlun Accompanied the Turkish Chargé d'Affaires to Beijing Yesterday

Li Jinlun, the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, is responsible for revising the Sino-Turkish Commercial Treaty. He came to Shanghai a few days ago to have contact with the Turkish Chargé d'Affaires, Fud Pei. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the Dutch Minister Oudenk visited him at the Foreign Affairs Discussion Meeting and discussed the treaty for 20 minutes before leaving. Mr. Li told this newspaper's reporter yesterday that the visit of Minister Oudenk was a normal social engagement. He plans to stay in Shanghai for a while. When Minister Wang comes to Shanghai this Saturday or Sunday, he will meet him in person and make some statements, and then return to Ping to handle matters. The draft of the Sino-Turkish Commercial Treaty has been prepared by our side. The Turkish Chargé d'Affaires, Fud Pei, will go to Beijing with me in the same car tonight (i.e., last night) to begin formal negotiations. As for the Sino-Finnish Commercial Treaty, both parties have agreed on a draft, and it is expected to be officially signed soon.

New Export Tariff Completely Drafted 141

Lower Taxes for Encouraged Exports

Higher Taxes for Restricted Exports

Xin Shanghai News reported that the new export tariff has been drafted by the National Tariff Commission. The reporter met with a member of the Tariff Commission yesterday and asked about the content of the new export tariff. According to him, the tariff was drafted after several days of mutual research by various specialized committee members. The content adopts a tiered taxation method. The tax rate for exports that should be encouraged is lower, and the tax rate for items that should be restricted from export is higher. Generally, 5% is still used as the basic tax rate, and then it is reviewed in light of the principles of the commercial treaties concluded with various countries before it can be determined.

Maze to Go to Hong Kong on a Fixed Date 142

To Discuss Establishing a Chinese Customs Inspection Branch in Hong Kong

Chief Inspector of Customs Maze is said to be leaving Shanghai on the 13th of this month to go to Hong Kong to discuss with the British authorities the establishment of a Chinese Customs inspection branch in Hong Kong in order to stop smuggling and increase national taxes. Since the implementation of the new tariff in China, smuggling has increased day by day, especially in Guangdong Province. Hong Kong, which is under British jurisdiction, is a free port and is only a short distance from Guangzhou, which makes it impossible to prevent smuggling and tax evasion. This has a great impact on China's tax revenue every year. Chief Inspector of Customs Maze, in view of this, once suggested to the government to establish a special department for anti-smuggling, the purpose of which was to focus on smuggling ships in Hong Kong and Taiwan. At that time, the government quite agreed with his proposal and ordered Maze to go to Hong Kong in person to discuss preventive measures with the British authorities. Therefore, Maze had a trip to Hong Kong last year. After negotiations, a draft customs agreement was drawn up. Unexpectedly, after the agreement was revised and agreed upon by both parties, the Chinese government had already approved it, but the British authorities used the excuse that Hong Kong ships had no right to navigate in the Chinese mainland and did not approve it. The regulations on navigation in the Chinese mainland stipulate that all ships navigating in the Chinese mainland must not sail to foreign ports. Since Hong Kong is under British jurisdiction, it is naturally one of the foreign ports. Therefore, the Chinese authorities are quite determined to maintain this point, and this agreement has been shelved until now. However, in the past year, smuggling has increased day by day. The Customs Administration has once again ordered Maze to go to Hong Kong to discuss this matter, in the hope that the agreement can be established as soon as possible and China's tax revenue can be maintained. If the British authorities intend to shirk their responsibility, the Chinese Customs will take strict measures, that is, to strictly monitor the four borders of Hong Kong, and to strictly inspect ships sailing into the Chinese seas from ports such as Hong Kong. It is also heard that Mr. Maze will go to Guangzhou, Xijiang and other ports this time to inspect business conditions, and will return to Shanghai in about three weeks.

Export 143

Boxed Tea Not Canceled, License Application for Tax Exemption

National Products Maintenance Association Sends Telegram to Ministry of Finance

The Chinese National Products Maintenance Association recently sent a special telegram to the Ministry of Finance regarding the export of boxed tea, which has not been canceled and applied for exemption from the main and half taxes. It stated that the association's member, the Shanghai Tea Guild, issued a public letter stating that the industry's export of boxed tea was exempt from taxes from August of the 8th year of the Republic. At that time, a guarantee was established that if the license was not canceled within a year, it would be treated as not having been exported and the main and half taxes should be paid. Various tea warehouses have never handled the procedures for canceling licenses and have been negligent, and even by the 14th year of the Republic, the Customs was urging the payment of taxes on licenses that had not been canceled. Six years have passed, and the tea warehouses have been destroyed twice in the meantime. How can the licenses be canceled? Moreover, during these years, foreign firms such as Meishi, Huili, Lutai, Guangda Kaili, Baoyuan, Gongmei, etc. have closed down and returned to their countries, and the original licenses cannot be found. Also, tea warehouses such as Wanhelong, Rongjixiang, Qiantai Changsen, Shengsheng Henglongtai Tongchun, Tongyixiang Qianshen, Anruichang Hengfengtai, etc. have gone bankrupt and returned to their hometowns, and the original licenses cannot be found. In addition, there are foreign firms that export without licenses. For example, if 1,000 dan are shipped out without a license, then 1,000 dan will be stored on the license. This is not an exaggeration, and there are letters from foreign firms to prove it. The above reasons are all true, and the tea leaves do not exist even though the licenses have not been canceled. Therefore, they requested the exemption from the Beijing Taxation Office at that time, but it was approved as an unsettled method, saying that exemptions would be granted before the 11th year of the Republic, and taxes would be paid according to the regulations after the 12th year. They planned to continue to apply for exemption, but the central government was established, and it was also put on hold. After another three years, no one mentioned it. It was only at the end of last year that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company inquired about the previous case and did not approve the cancellation and should continue to pay. Therefore, this time, the Ministry of Finance's request for exemption was not approved. However, we can only rely on your association to verify the facts, which are all true, and the tea industry is in a desperate situation. For the sake of expanding exports, the government is planning various reward measures, and how can it bear to be stingy with this small amount and investigate the past? In the government's efforts to encourage exports, all foreign tea exports are exempt from taxes and levies, and there are various subsidies, so they can be very developed and seize our Hua tea's great profits. Merchants have a conscience and are afraid to make extra demands because the government has difficulties. However, this tax arrears cannot be investigated, and it is difficult to compensate, so we have no choice but to hope that the government will consider the situation, and please ask your association to add a note on behalf of the Ministry of Finance, approving the exemption of the main and half taxes on the licenses for green tea that have not been canceled before the 18th year. From the 19th year onwards, if there are overdue and uncanceled licenses, they must be paid in accordance with the regulations. Over the meeting, according to this, the industry has suffered from foreign tea oppression and sluggish foreign sales in recent years and has barely maintained it to this day, and feels deeply exhausted. The various reasons for the uncanceled licenses stated by the guild are true. In order to protect Chinese tea, we sincerely hope that your ministry will grant exemption from the main and half taxes on the said uncanceled licenses from this year, and must pay in accordance with the regulations from this year onwards, so as to alleviate the merchants' difficulties and assist in maintaining the industry. We cannot bear the urgency and anticipation of it, and please instruct us to obey, which is a virtue. Wang Jiean, Wang Xingyi, and Wang Hanqiang, standing committee members of the Chinese National Products Maintenance Association, kowtowed.

Question of Cocoon Insurance Rate 145

Insurance Companies Insist on Following New Regulations

Due to a Loss of More Than 40,000 Taels Last Year

The Shanghai Insurance Association, a member of various insurance companies, held a temporary meeting at the Zilin newspaper office at noon yesterday to make a final discussion on the issue of cocoon insurance rates. The reason is that last year, due to the low insurance premiums and the unstable political situation, the entire insurance industry actually lost more than 40,000 taels. This year, bandits are rampant in the inland, which is even more terrifying. Therefore, the implementation of the new regulations is feared to suffer even greater losses, and all manufacturers have been notified to check.

Shanghai Local Court 150

Yesterday's Swearing-In of the Chief Judge and Prosecutor

The swearing-in ceremony for Shen Bingqian, the Chief Judge of the Shanghai Local Court, and Liu Maochu, the Chief Prosecutor, was held yesterday morning at 10:00 AM in the First Tribunal, concluding at 12:00 PM. The details are recorded below:

Guests: The supervising officials present were Shen Yuan, Presiding Judge of the High Court, and Zhong Shangbin, Prosecutor of the High Procuratorate. Party representatives present were Pan Gongzhan. Special district Local Court officials present were Yang Zhaosun, Chief Judge, and Zhou Xianjue, Chief Prosecutor; Wang Zhennan, Chief Prosecutor of the Second Branch of the High Court; Mei Guangfu, Warden of the Second Prison. In total, there were over two hundred employees of the court. Chief Judge Shen Bingqian presided over the ceremony.

Order: The order of the ceremony was as follows: (1) Supervising officials take their seats. (2) Chief Judge takes his seat. (3) Chief Prosecutor takes his seat. (4) All stand at attention. (5) Sing the Party Song. (6) Offer the highest respect to the Party, the National Flag, and the portrait of the Premier. (7) The Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's Will. (8) Observe three minutes of silence. (9) Chief Judge takes the oath. (10) Chief Prosecutor takes the oath. (11) Supervising officials deliver instructions. (12) Party representative delivers a speech. (13) Guests deliver speeches. (14) Chief Judge gives a response. (15) Chief Prosecutor gives a response. (16) Ceremony concludes with a photograph.

Oath: The oath is recorded below. I, (name), hereby swear that I will strictly adhere to the Premier's will, obey the Party's principles, abide by the national laws and regulations, be loyal and diligent in my duties, and economize on expenses. I vow never to employ useless personnel, engage in personal gain or corruption, or accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment from the Party.

Instructions: "Instructions from Shen Yuan, representative of the Jiangsu High Court President": Now is a period of political tutelage, and also when we have recovered extraterritoriality rights. The quality of the court's handling of matters truly carries immense weight. The court is the agency to protect human rights, and judges hold the power to administer impartial justice, which concerns the lives and property of the people. It should be handled according to law and not be neglected. All colleagues should be honest and self-disciplined, and strive to do better. If the authorities can put in more effort, lawsuits and injustices can be reduced, and the people can have more happiness. Shanghai is a major commercial port where Chinese and foreigners reside together, and the number of cases is much greater than in other courts. The selection of the Chief Judge is of utmost importance. Chief Judge Shen has served in the legal field for many years, and his knowledge and experience are both excellent. As the former Chief Prosecutor of the Shanghai court, he is already experienced. Now that former Chief Judge Yang has been transferred to the special district court, the Ministry has promoted Chief Judge Shen to fill the vacancy. This is a manifestation of the emphasis on talent. It is hoped that Chief Judge Shen will, together with the staff, follow the teachings of the late Premier, possess a spirit of fearlessness, not be afraid of difficulties, not be complacent, and conscientiously reorganize and actively revitalize the court, setting an example for all courts, and bringing a unique brilliance to the Jiangsu judicial system. This is what the President deeply expects. "Instructions from Zhong Shangbin, representative of the Jiangsu High Court Chief Prosecutor": Today is the date of the swearing-in ceremony for Chief Prosecutor Liu and Chief Judge Shen of the Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court. I, Shangbin, was commissioned by Chief Wang of the Jiangsu High Court to represent him in supervising the ceremony. I am very pleased to be able to participate in this grand event. Shanghai is the most important commercial area of our country. In the past, under the oppression of foreign nations, the consular jurisdiction system was established, infringing upon our national sovereignty. Now that consular jurisdiction has just been recovered, the international status of our nation has been slightly restored. However, the special spirit of our nation has not yet been promoted. Everyone serving in domestic institutions must fulfill this responsibility, especially those serving in the Shanghai judicial institutions, which are observed by foreign nations. They must fulfill this responsibility even more. Chief Prosecutor Liu graduated from the University of Lyon in France and has a profound understanding of law. Now that consular jurisdiction has been recovered, he shoulders this important mission and will surely promote the spirit of our nation, preserve and enhance our nation's inherent morality and intelligence. Chief Judge Shen has long been in charge of prosecution affairs at the Shanghai court, and his character and learning are both excellent, which I have always admired. Now that Chief Prosecutor Liu and Chief Judge Shen are working together in one place, they will surely cooperate sincerely and complement each other. I hope that Chief Prosecutor Liu will pay attention to the three words "清慎勤" (integrity, prudence, and diligence) in his duties and encourage himself with them.

Speech: Pan Gongzhan stated briefly, "I am very pleased to participate in the ceremony for Chief Judge Shen and Chief Prosecutor Liu today because Chief Judge Shen has served as Chief Prosecutor in Shanghai for many years, and the new Chief Prosecutor is also very knowledgeable in law. With his experience and knowledge, I am confident that he will be able to cope with the affairs of Shanghai society. Therefore, we are very satisfied. According to Mr. Wang Yunwu's research on the increase in population and crime at the Central Research Institute, the increase in population in Shanghai is unparalleled in the world, but the number of criminals has also increased at the same time. Therefore, a village of several hundred people cannot be compared to a city of several hundred thousand people. Shanghai has a population of over 2.8 million, and a few years ago it was 2 million. According to his research, the increase in crime is faster than the increase in population, resulting in more criminals. To remedy this, on the one hand, education must be provided to bring people back on the right track, and on the other hand, economic development and industrial projects must be undertaken to prevent panic about food, clothing, and housing. However, this is a fundamental solution. On the other hand, a symptomatic solution is also needed because before the fundamental solution is found, there should be no leniency towards those who have committed crimes, and they must be dealt with strictly in order to reduce the number of offenders. Regarding the symptomatic solution, we cannot help but hope that the court... some say that party rule and the rule of law are in conflict, but this is completely wrong. We must use the Party's principles to legislate, which is the so-called Party's rule of law. We hope that the gentlemen in the judicial field will not forget the Party's principles when reporting and enforcing the law, that is, to deal severely with the communist reactionary elements who do all kinds of evil deeds because they oppose the Party and violate the law. Because they are cruel and have no feelings, they want to revolt against the Kuomintang and the country, and give China away to Russia. I have high hopes for these two gentlemen. I am straightforward, so I say whatever I think of, to contribute to the public."

Response: "Chief Judge Shen's Response" briefly stated that the instructions from the superiors and the guidance from the Party representatives were very detailed regarding the judicial aspect. I am aware of my own weakness and will work harder in the future. Speaking of judicial independence, it does not mean that everyone is independent. Judicial independence cannot be achieved without the support of all courts. In fact, the judiciary is not the judiciary of one person, but is established by the state for the people and for all the people. Those in the judicial field should not think that since I am in the judicial field, the judiciary is mine, because that will not work. Today, doing things in the judicial field means being the judiciary. Not doing things in the judicial field means being like ordinary people. It is difficult to have every judicial official agree on everything, but as long as everyone is loyal to their duties and walks the same path, they must understand that the judiciary is for the benefit of all the people. That is what I mean. I am weak, so I feel apprehensive. Fortunately, there are wise officials to supervise me, and I have served in Shanghai for many years, and I rarely interact with people outside. In the future, if there is anything I do not do well, I hope to be guided. Today's hospitality is simple, I hope you will forgive me, and so on. "Chief Prosecutor Liu's Response" briefly stated that I am very honored by everyone's presence today. A country has rights both internally and externally, and the judiciary is one of the internal rights. Judicial independence does not mean going beyond national sovereignty. In the third and fourth years of the Republic of China, the Beijing Ministry of Justice repeatedly prohibited judicial officials from joining the Party, but the judiciary is a kind of spirit and is not interfered with because of a person's party membership. Judicial officials should act according to the Party's program and principles, and the country will achieve peace. Therefore, I hope that judicial officials will run into the Kuomintang position and work hard. I hope that our colleagues will work hard together.
