Public Concession 153

Streetcar Strike Update

The streetcar strike in the Public Concession has lasted for nine days. Not only the public feels inconvenienced, but the company is also very anxious. After negotiations with the compradore Mr. Hu broke down, the company issued a notice on the afternoon of the 5th, stating that ticket sellers and drivers could receive a daily allowance of ten cents, as well as a subsidy of three dollars. It also announced that work would resume on the morning of the 6th. Upon hearing this, the strike committee and all the workers, starting early in the morning of the 6th, dozens of strike committee members went separately to the Shanghai East, Shanghai West, Zhabei three district offices and news outposts to report the above news to the workers and solicit their opinions. By 6:00 PM, dozens of committee members had returned to the presidium office, reporting on the situation of the workers in each district. Yesterday, there were twelve mass meetings. In addition, at each news outpost (there are more than ten), there were nineteen to twenty people gathered to talk to the strike committee members and report important news to them. The presidium of the strike committee immediately passed the following resolutions: (1) The company's announcement is completely deceiving and insulting to the workers, because (a) the subsidy of three dollars is completely empty talk. Is the subsidy a subsidy for wage losses during the strike period, or a subsidy for other losses? Moreover, the subsidy may be given today but not tomorrow. (b) The three-dollar subsidy for ticket sellers and drivers has nothing to do with the coppersmiths, specialists, lamplighters, road workers, etc. Isn't this dividing our workers' solidarity? Therefore, we should insist on the strike and strive for the thirteen demands. (2) Anyone who drives the streetcars first, whether a Chinese lackey or a foreign scab, and undermines the strike will be severely dealt with. (3) Intensify organizational work, propaganda work, patrol team work, and news gathering work. We will not resume work until we achieve victory.

Chinese and Foreign Shipping Companies 154

Actively Expanding Yangtze River Shipping

The slump in Yangtze River shipping has reached its extreme recently. There is a shortage of both incoming and outgoing goods. Due to the sluggish business, various companies are seeking remedial measures, such as lowering shipping rates and building more fast ships, all in order to gain an advantage. During this period of sluggish business, Chinese and foreign shipping companies are making fundamental reforms to improve the situation. Planning ahead is the key to business competition and demonstrates the foreign merchants' painstaking efforts and full dedication to operating on the Yangtze River route. The situation of the competition between Chinese and foreign ships is described separately below:

China Merchants Group Developing Business: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's eight Yangtze River ships have not been able to fully resume service for a long time. This time, the headquarters ordered the Jian Guo, Jiang Xin, and others to be returned. Six ships have now been confirmed to be sailing on the Yangtze River route. The four major Yangtze River ships (Jiang Shun, Jiang An, Jiang Hua, and Jiang Xin) will be running on a regular schedule starting this month. The business department has finalized the regulations, and each ship will run at least sixteen times a month. The above number of trips has been scheduled for May. When the Jiang Yu ship returns to Shanghai, the number of trips can be increased to nineteen times a month. If each ship carries an average of 5,000 taels worth of cargo and passengers back and forth, the monthly income on the Yangtze River route will be over 100,000 taels. This is the month with the most Yangtze River liners for the company since April last year. If the sailing schedule is accurate, the business will naturally improve.

Chinese and Foreign Competition for Passengers: After the dissolution of the Public Ticket Bureau, most foreign ships took back the ticketing rights for themselves. Although Chinese Yangtze River ships are still contracted by business managers, first-class tickets are also owned by the company. Last month, foreign Yangtze River ships planned to take advantage of the gold price increase to increase fares. At that time, it had already been proposed, but it was opposed by the Chinese merchants when soliciting the consent of the Chinese ships, so the price increase was invisibly canceled. It is now heard that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has signed a sales agency contract with the China Travel Service for Yangtze River downstream passenger tickets in order to expand its passenger business as much as possible.

British Merchants Urgently Building New Ships: In recent years, fast ships have become popular in the shipping industry. Those that have a high speed and can reach their destination quickly will surely have good business. The British company Jardine Matheson in this port has already built two fast motor ships for use on the Yangtze River. One ship, the Wuhu, which operates on the upper reaches, will soon come to Shanghai to start service. One ship, which operates on the Shanghai-Hankou route, is also under construction. Each ship can travel at a speed of over fourteen nautical miles per hour. Jardine Matheson is also building a fast ship in a shipyard in this port, using a motor engine. It is said that the construction will be completed soon, and the name of the ship has been determined, seemingly as the "Sheng He," which is prepared to compete in the business on this route. This year, it will also be able to sail. The day when each of these new ships is completed will be the beginning of competition for Yangtze River shipping.

Foreign Ships Fully Open on the Upper Reaches: Foreign ships on the upper Yangtze River went on strike starting March 20th to resist the increase in wages for the river pilots. At that time, twenty-eight ships suspended operations. Later, the Jijiang and Nissin companies were the first to individually agree to the wage increase. On April 20th, American and Japanese ships first departed from Shanghai for Chongqing to resume service. British Jardine Matheson ships also went to Yichang to wait for the resumption of service. As for the Taikoo company, it has a total of eight ships operating on the Yichang-Chongqing route. After the suspension of service, most of them returned to Shanghai. Now, a telegram has been received from Yichang, saying that the wage increase conditions have been agreed upon, and the river pilots have all boarded the ships. Therefore, the Wanxian, Wantong, Wanliu, and other ships in Shanghai have all received orders to sail. They will load large quantities of cotton yarn in this port and go directly to Chongqing. They can all sail upstream before the 11th. From today onwards, there will be thirty-nine ships operating on the Chongqing route, and Chinese merchant ships will only account for eight of them.

Embezzlement of Compensation for May 30th Massacre 156

Some People Heartlessly Claiming Compensation

Martyrs' Grievances Buried Underground

Claimants Without Conscience

Authorities Should Punish Severely

The May 30th Massacre occurred several years ago. It was not until the end of last year, after repeated negotiations, that a portion of the compensation was obtained from the Municipal Council and distributed to the families of the victims. Unexpectedly, the embezzlement of compensation has recently occurred. A lawsuit has been filed in the Special District Local Court. The plaintiffs are Hu Changsheng and Chen Fucai, representatives of the May 30th Massacre Victims' Families Association. The defendants are Xu Zhijian, owner of the Zhichengtai Tea Shop at 152 Maode Road, Xiaoshadu, and Li Ruiqing, Wang Zhaohua, He Hanwen, and others, members of the internal and external cotton mill workers' union. According to the plaintiffs' complaint, the association distributed compensation to the victims' families on January 25th of this year. Considering that most of them were from other provinces and were not familiar with each other, the association repeatedly stated that it would not issue compensation unless the family members came to the association in person and had a shop guarantee. The procedures were thorough and careful. Unexpectedly, a person claiming to be Luo Wenlang, the elder brother of the victim Luo Wenzhao, came to the association accompanied by Li Ruiqing, Wang Zhaohua, He Hanwen, and others to register with a guarantee from Zhichengtai Tea Shop, requesting compensation of 2,000 yuan. The association verified that there was no error and immediately paid the compensation. Recently, Luo Wenlang filed a complaint with the Municipal Party Department, alleging that the compensation he received did not match the amount reported in the newspaper and requested an investigation. The Municipal Party Department transferred the case to the Municipal Government for investigation. The case is serious, and the association has also conducted a thorough investigation. The guarantor has already fled the shop. The case involves colluding with the guarantor to fraudulently obtain compensation, which constitutes the crime of fraudulently obtaining property. It violates criminal law and damages the national image. If it is not dealt with promptly, the suspects will surely escape without a trace. Therefore, the plaintiffs request that the defendants be immediately arrested and brought to justice. Upon receiving the complaint, the court issued summonses, ordering the Huisi Police Station to notify the defendants to appear in court for trial yesterday afternoon. When the time came, Judge Wu Tingqi opened the court. Xu Zhijian, the owner of Zhicheng Tea Shop, claimed to have a heart pain and was accompanied by his wife, Xu Jiangshi, and a representative lawyer. The other three defendants, Li, Wang, and He, had all fled and were not present. According to the plaintiff Hu Changsheng's statement, the 2,000 yuan compensation was issued on December 28th of the lunar calendar. Luo Wenlang claimed that he only received 240 yuan, but the receipt he issued was for 500 yuan, and so on. Judge Wu stated that the witnesses were not all present and could not proceed. He ordered the defendants to be summoned in person and rescheduled the hearing.

Rampant Pirates 157

Severely Affecting the Fish Market

The Jin Changtai Boat Was the Most Miserable

Not a Single Fish or Grain of Rice Left

The Crew Has Been Starving for Two Whole Days

The Ferocity of the Pirates Is Evident

The spring fish market in Wusong has always been the best of commerce in the entire town. Not only do those in the fish business rely on it to make a living, but many Hakka people from Qingkou, Shandong, and Yancheng, Jiangsu, also use it to make a living. Every year after the Qingming Festival, they arrive in Wusong one after another to gather and wait for fishing boats to enter the port so that they can be active. The total amount of business is over 500,000 yuan each year, excluding the fish and small goods sold by the fishing boat crews themselves, which are sold through the Cuisheng, Binfeng, and Shentai firms. In previous years, the number of boats arriving has been about a hundred in the first catch and at least a hundred in the second catch, with as many as two or three hundred boats. Unexpectedly, this year, more than a hundred pirate ships and five hundred pirates were found in the fishing waters. Relying on their sophisticated firearms, they wreaked havoc, either robbing ships and goods, or kidnapping people for ransom. Those with cash were required to pay 80 yuan per ship to obtain a white flag from the Qinghuai gang pirate leader Shen Guanxi (with a large fish character in the middle of the flag and the words "Public Charity Organization" on the side). Only then would they be allowed to fish. However, there are very few ships with cash. As a result, less than forty fishing boats arrived in Wusong for the first catch. The largest and most famous fish market in Jiangsu Province is Wusong, followed by Liuhe, and then the Pengjia Bridge in the jurisdiction of Hupu. It is said that only two fishing boats arrived at Pengjia Bridge, which shows the decline of its business. Currently, less than thirty boats have arrived in Wusong for the second catch. The fish they have caught only fill one hold or half a hold, and the rest has been robbed. What those pirates pay most attention to are the defensive guns and cannons on the boats. All those that have them are robbed. The most tragic was the Jin Changtai boat that arrived in Wusong yesterday morning. Not only was there not a single fish left, but also not a grain of rice. Even the firewood, rice, clothes, and bedding brought by the boat were searched and robbed without leaving anything. Not yet satisfied, they kidnapped three crew members, claiming that they had to prepare 10,000 yuan to ransom the hostages. Because the boat had run out of food, it sailed to Wusong specifically. They had not had a meal for two whole days on the way. When they arrived in Wusong, the Cuisheng fish firm immediately sent a load of rice to the boat, and the crew was able to have a full meal. According to Wang, the supervisor of the anti-smuggling battalion's patrol boat No. 2, he saw that the boat had been completely searched and robbed of everything except the boat equipment. The tragic situation was truly heartbreaking. Currently, because the pirates are so rampant, the spring fish market has become disintegrated. Not only is the customs revenue greatly affected, but the capital of the three firms is also at stake. When spring fish boats go to sea, they prepare expenses from the fish firms, at least 200 yuan per boat, and as much as 500 or 600 yuan. When the fish are caught and sold in Wusong, the money is deducted. They get commissions and can recover the loans. This has always been the case. Unexpectedly, this year, not only is there no commission, but also the capital has become a bubble. In recent days, the managers of the fish firms have been crestfallen and deeply worried. Another saying is that a famous Zhao (not a pirate) in the Huaixuhai gang expressed opposition to Shen Guanxi, and any fishing boat with Shen's flag was not allowed to fish. Therefore, the fishermen felt that there was no way out. If the pirates are so ferocious and this continues, the fishermen's suffering is unknown.

Suicide Attempt by a Couple in the New Jiangsu Hotel 159

Woman Dead, Man Detained by Police

Two guests, a man and a woman, checked into room 30 of the New Jiangsu Hotel at 295 Hubei Road a few days ago. The man, named Zhang Zhiyun, was 27 years old and from Hangzhou. The woman, named Zhang Jinbao, was 27 years old and from Pinghu. The man was dressed fashionably and looked like a middle-class businessman. The woman had a bob haircut and wore leather shoes, and looked like a young woman from a wealthy family. However, when they checked in, they both looked worried. The service staff often saw this kind of expression on guests, so they didn't pay much attention. Around 5:00 AM yesterday morning, panting sounds were frequently heard from their room. The tea attendant knew that something was wrong and wanted to knock on the door to see what was happening, but there was no response after knocking several times. The tea attendant urgently reported to the front desk. They pried open the door and saw the man and woman lying stiffly on the bed with pale faces. The hotel reported the incident to the Laozha Police Station, and detective Zhao Ziren rushed to investigate. He saw that Zhang Jinbao was barely breathing and Zhang Zhiyun was still able to speak. Two cigarette paper bags were found next to him. According to him, he was working at Yuhexing at 233 Xinmatou in Nanshi. Recently, he had become addicted to gambling and went to a gambling den in the French Concession every day, resulting in a large debt that he was too ashamed to face people. Therefore, he wanted to commit suicide by swallowing raw opium. The female guest, Zhang Jinbao, was Zhiyun's mistress. Seeing Zhang taking poison, she decided to die with him to show her determination, and so on. They were sent to Renji Hospital by a Chinese police car for treatment. The doctor said that the woman had taken a large dose of poison and was unlikely to survive, while the man could still be saved. Zhang Jinbao died yesterday afternoon. The police sent the body to the forensic examination office on Fielun Road and scheduled a report to the Special District Court to come to the scene for examination today. Zhang Zhiyun took a lighter dose of poison and was temporarily detained by the police yesterday afternoon. They plan to interrogate him together today.

Da Sheng Cotton Mill Employee 160

Schemes to Defraud a Large Sum

Feigning Madness, Falls into a Dung Pit

A Large Amount of Banknotes Hidden Underground

Defrauds 2,000 Yuan in Nantong

Escapes to Shanghai, Ultimately Arrested

Last year, the Da Sheng Cotton Mill in Nantong had 6,000 yuan in cash stolen. At the time, Shen Zelin, an employee of the mill from Haimen, suddenly appeared to be insane, behaving erratically. One day, he even fell into a dung pit. The mill's management initially did not suspect any connection between this behavior and the theft of the money. However, after some time, they began to suspect that Shen's madness was a pretense, intended to cover up the crime. After severe questioning, Shen confessed, admitting that he had hidden the stolen money underground in the mill's garden. A search was conducted, and 4,500 yuan was recovered. The remaining 1,500 yuan had been spent. Shen was fired, and the guarantor compensated for the missing amount. The matter was then put to rest. However, on April 30th of this year, Shen suddenly went to the Da Sheng Cotton Mill in Shanglinsha, claiming to be the manager sent by the Nantong Da Sheng Cotton Mill to audit the accounts. Han Jiping, the director of Da Sheng in Shanglinsha, initially treated him hospitably. When Shen requested 2,000 yuan, Han stated that they would need to go to the main factory in Nantong for verification. Shen agreed, but requested the money in advance. Han, believing that there would be no problem since they were going together, paid the full amount. They then traveled to Nantong. As they approached a middle school in front of the main factory, Shen claimed that his younger brother was studying there and asked to go into the school to visit him, requesting Han to wait outside. After Shen entered the school, Han waited for a long time, but Shen did not come out. It turned out that he had seized the opportunity to escape. Han reported the incident to the main factory, which then reported it to the local Public Security Bureau for investigation. It was discovered that Shen had taken a ship to Shanghai and was hiding in room 317 of the Dongya Hotel. The factory sent Cai Junhe and another person to Shanghai to report to the Lao Zha Gate Police Station. Detective Wang Yingjie arrested Shen Zelin at 9:00 AM the day before. A passbook from the China Industrial Bank with a balance of 1,400 yuan, as well as 130 yuan in cash, were confiscated. The following morning, Shen was taken to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Xu interrogated him and ordered him to be detained pending further investigation by the Nantong Local Court.

Body Recovered

He has been a driver at New Chang for three years without any faults. Recently, there was no difference.

Page 16

There was no sign of mental illness. However, twelve hours before the drowning, he told the ship's first mate that his mind was already lost and he would die soon, so he wanted to drown himself. The first mate tried to comfort him and persuaded him not to have such thoughts. Chen Fusheng insisted that the drowning was his own will and could sign a letter as proof to the first mate. Later, he told the head of the sailors that he wanted to drown himself because his mind was lost and he could not survive. After the head persuaded him repeatedly to rest, the head sent someone to Chen's bunk twice to see if he was safely in bed, so the sailors felt relieved and went to sleep themselves. Unexpectedly, at around 12:00 midnight, Chen took advantage of everyone's sleep to sneak out and drown himself. At that time, a small boat selling goods was docked outside the New Chang ship. They knew that he had drowned and immediately tried to retrieve him, but his body was nowhere to be found. The search continued for half a day the next day, but there was no sign of him. The New Chang then returned to Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai yesterday, the crew notified his family and reported to the head office. It was heard that the head office received a telegram from Guangzhou yesterday, saying that Chen Fusheng's body had been recovered by the Guangdong Provincial Water Police and will be transported to Shanghai after burial. Yesterday afternoon, Chen's wife and children came to the ship to inquire about the truth of the matter.

Zhu Chen 166

Drowned in a Boiling Water Pot and Died

Zhu Xuegen, 40 years old, from Yancheng, Jiangbei, was a cleaner at the Municipal Health Bureau. His wife, Chen, was 38 years old. They lived together in a thatched house at No. 6 Jianyu Lane, Hainan West Alley, South Street, outside Xiaonanmen, South City. Zhu was overjoyed because his wife, who had never had children, was suddenly pregnant. On the 29th of last month, Mao, the wife of their co-resident Liu Dengji, set up a stove outside the thatched house to cook because the house was too small. After pouring boiling water into the pot, she went inside to fetch something. Zhu's wife, Chen, remembered that her shoes were drying on the roof of the thatched house and wanted to take them down quickly. However, because the house was high and she was short, she could not reach them. So, she used a wooden stool to elevate herself. As she reached out to retrieve the shoes, Liu's wife, Mao, carrying something, suddenly walked out from inside. In the rush, she accidentally bumped into Chen, causing Chen to lose her balance and fall into the pot of boiling water. Instantly, her whole body was scalded. When she was pulled up, her skin was red and blistered, and she fainted from the pain. Zhu immediately sent her to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. However, because the injuries were too severe, she showed no improvement after several days. So, she was taken home the day before, and she died that evening. Zhu believed that his wife's death was entirely Liu's wife's fault. He immediately grabbed Liu and handed her over to Fan Shiqing, the security guard at the 26th post, who brought her back to the First District, Third Precinct. Chief Jin ordered an interrogation. Because it was a matter of life and death, he ordered that the suspect be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court along with the original documents for investigation.

Yong'an Tugboat 167

Sailor Tragically Drowned

During the fishing season, the Wusong Yunzao Creek has been a place where fishing boats from various gangs dock and unload. In recent days, there have been more than a hundred fishing boats coming to Wusong, so that the port surface is full of masts and sails and is extremely crowded. Yesterday morning at around 11:00, the Yan Cheng Gang chief manager of Bao Feng Fish Shop, Dong Lu Qing, the Tong Chang Tai and Gong Fa Sheng Wang De Shun and other three fishing boats were towed into the Wusong estuary by the Hua Fa small steamer and slowly sailed into the Yunzao Creek. They were planning to choose a location to anchor and dock when the Changshun tugboat of Yong'an Cotton Mill and two other small steamers were nearby. Seeing the fishing boat approaching, fearing that the two sides would collide and cause a disaster, they immediately gave way. Unexpectedly, during the turning of the Changshun tugboat, the stern of the boat went under the hawser of the Tong Chang Tai fishing boat. Jiang Zhihai, the deputy fireman of the boat, who was standing at the stern of the boat working, did not notice it and was knocked into the water. By the time the crew realized it, it was impossible to rescue him because the river was deep and the water was rapid and the boats were crowded. Jiang was 38 years old and from Nantong. He had an old mother and wife at home who depended on Jiang for their livelihood. He had been the deputy fireman on the tugboat for only three weeks and was tragically killed. Afterwards, Dong Lu Qing, the manager of Bao Feng Fish Shop, feeling sorry for Jiang's family, donated 70 yuan to be used for compensation. He also reported to the Lifeboat Bureau, asking them to send patrol boats to try to recover the body. Until yesterday evening, the body had not been found.

Maid Commits Suicide Out of Weariness of the World 168

Because Her Home Was Robbed Clean by Bandits

Weng Nianqu, the owner of Tong Feng Yong Silver Shop, located at the Parachute Ground, Nanjing Road, lived at No. 9 Weihe Lane, Zhao Fang Lane, West Gate, South City. Several months ago, he hired a maid from Luxu named Zhuang, about 40 years old. Yesterday morning at around 7:00, Zhuang suddenly hanged herself in the small room across from the kitchen of Weng's house. By the time someone noticed, she had been dead for a long time. Her body was cold to the touch. The matter was immediately reported to Chief Qian of the Second District, First Precinct of the Shenxiangge police station. Hearing the news, Chief Qian, considering it a matter of life and death, personally led Inspector Qiang Yude and Patrol Chief Wang Yufan to the scene for a detailed investigation. They saw a white cloth belt tied to the door of the deceased's bedroom. The deceased's neck also had a strip of cloth tied around it. According to Weng Nianqu, the deceased had not been here for long. However, when she first arrived, she claimed that her hometown of Luxu had been robbed clean by bandits and she often spoke of being weary of the world. The reason for her suicide was likely because of this. After finishing his statement, Chief Qian immediately ordered the local security to report to the court for inspection. At 4:00 in the afternoon, the court dispatched Prosecutor Guai, along with a clerk, to the scene to conduct a clear inspection. It was determined that she had committed suicide by hanging. He ordered the body to be handled by the corpse owner Weng Nianqu and ordered Weng to notify the Fang surname headman to promptly inform the deceased's family.

Regular Price-Controlled Rice Sales at Caojiadu 169

Shanghai Special City Social Affairs Bureau, because rice prices have soared, and the poor have suffered significant damage, has been planning to establish a price-controlled rice bureau to implement price-controlled rice sales to help the poor. It has been decided that starting from the 10th of this month, price-controlled rice sales will be implemented at the Caojiadu, located in the west of Shanghai, a vast area with a large number of poor people. The price is set at 14 yuan and 5 jiao per stone. Each poor person is limited to one sheng to five sheng per day, from 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM and from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM. Preparations have already begun.

Taxi Fares Will Increase 170

Resolved by a Joint Meeting Yesterday

The Shanghai Taxi Association held a general meeting at the Dengtuomo Hotel yesterday afternoon. Representatives from 57 companies including Yunfei, Lili, Tanle, Public, Global, Allenpas, Huishan, and Hui were present. During the meeting, Secretary Sheng Xiegui first reported on the association's affairs, saying that there were already 95 members this year, an increase of more than 40 companies compared to last winter, accounting for nine-tenths of all taxi companies in Shanghai. In the future, he hoped that members would work hard to introduce new members. Next, new staff were elected. Then, association affairs were discussed. It was said that recently, the expenses of each company, including house donations, correspondence, insurance fees, stamp taxes, etc., have been greatly increased. Now, tires and gasoline have also increased in price one after another. If the car rental is not increased appropriately, it is difficult to maintain business. It was resolved that, on the one hand, the car rental will be increased, and on the other hand, a cash payment system for car rental will be implemented to maintain the capital. The detailed method will be discussed by the association's committee. It is expected that the price increase method will be announced soon.

Pujiang Ferry 171

Recruiting Trainees, Advance Notice

Issuing Regulations, Regularly Recruiting

Since the Shanghai Municipal Pujiang Ferry has been taken over by the Municipal Public Utility Bureau, its business has been developing rapidly. The current original routes are being expanded, and cross-river ferries will also be realized. There is a great need for talent in all affairs and navigation aspects. In order to cultivate talent in advance to meet future needs, it is planned to recruit twelve trainees. After being admitted, they will be assigned to the ferry management office and various ferries to practice for one to two years. After the end of the period, they will be appointed to appropriate positions. The Bureau has now drawn up the regulations and submitted them to the municipal government for approval. Once the recruitment period is set, a notice will be published in the newspaper. The regulations are recorded as follows: (1) The Pujiang Ferry Management Office of this Bureau recruits twelve trainees for the purpose of training ferry management personnel, divided into (A) navigation, (B) mechanical affairs (C) administrative services, four for each type. (2) Applicants must have no bad habits, be in good health, be of upright character, and be between the ages of eighteen and twenty-five. Applicants for navigation or administrative services must also have a junior high school education or equivalent. Applicants for mechanical affairs must have a junior high school education or equivalent and have considerable technical knowledge. (3) Applicants must fill out a brief resume, along with a recent four-inch half-length photo, and submit it to the Bureau for review and regular examination. (4) Those who pass the examination must fill out a letter of intent, find a guarantor, and report to the Bureau for registration and assignment to the ferry management office and various ferries for practice. (5) The internship period is one to two years. Those who achieve excellent results at the end of the period will be appointed to appropriate positions by the Bureau and paid according to regulations. In addition to the provision of food, lodging, and uniforms by the Bureau during the internship period, each person will receive a discretionary allowance. (6) During the internship period, if trainees disobey orders or violate regulations and are expelled by the Bureau, or if they drop out without reason, they must return the uniform fee and allowance and compensate the Bureau for food and lodging expenses, calculated at fifteen yuan per month. (7) After the trainees complete their studies and are assigned to positions, they should serve on the ferry for at least one to two years. Those who resign midway will be handled in accordance with Article 6.

Western Newspaper on 172

Comments on the Leprosy Relief Society

The *North China Daily News* said that leprosy is the most disgusting disease and many people do not want to mention it. However, the proper way is to take positive measures to make this fierce devil disappear permanently. Moreover, leprosy is not an incurable disease. If treated early, it can be completely eradicated. Therefore, we should do our best to assist institutions that provide leprosy relief, regardless of their size. Poor hygiene is the only cause of leprosy. The Chinese environment is the most suitable for the breeding of bacteria. (According to surveys, there are one million lepers in China.) In addition, frequent civil wars have made the government take no measures for leprosy. Not only are there no appropriate hospitals to accommodate patients, but there is also a lack of widespread publicity about the dangers of leprosy. Other things, such as isolating the children of patients and encouraging patients to seek medical treatment voluntarily, are beyond the reach of dreams. Therefore, under these circumstances, the work of eradicating leprosy depends on the promotion of enthusiastic people. The Chinese Leprosy Relief Society is dedicated to eradicating leprosy in China. Since its establishment, it has achieved remarkable results. Taking Shanghai as an example, it has spared no effort in investigating and treating patients, benefiting the sick greatly. It is also connected with the World Leprosy Relief Society, the American Leprosy Relief Society, the International Leprosy Alliance, and the Ministry of Health of the National Government. Branches have been established in Hong Kong, Fuzhou, and other places. Furthermore, the establishment of leprosy hospitals in various places is under planning. However, such undertakings require huge expenses. Without the concerted efforts of everyone, it is difficult to achieve success. We hope that people from all walks of life will provide practical assistance and not regard it as an ordinary organization.

Song Lanhui Married a Wife 173

Has Another Relationship with Another Girl

Acidity Causes Waves, and the Law Deals With It

Song Zhou, also known as Zhou Meiqing, a young woman from Haimen, 25 years old, lives in the Shanghai Yarn Factory residential area on Pingliang Road. In the spring of the 15th year of the Republic of China, she married Song Ganfei, also known as Song Lanhui, a fellow villager who worked as a car driver, through her parents' orders and a matchmaker's words. After marriage, they were initially harmonious. A few months later, Lanhui had a relationship with another young woman. Meiqing heard about it and caused a storm of jealousy. The couple then became estranged and did not come home to stay. Even if they met, they were like thorns in each other's eyes. During this period, Song Lanhui did not provide for the family. The woman had to work at the yarn factory, and the wages she earned were used to temporarily cover the household's needs. Recently, things have become even more intensified, with frequent quarrels and beatings. Yesterday, she hired a lawyer to deal with her husband through legal means. The purpose of the request is to demand cohabitation or compensation for corresponding living expenses. After the husband found out the bottom line, he also hired a lawyer to refute it. The two sides are currently in negotiations.

Husband Addicted to Gambling, Wife Takes Poison 174

Body Still Needs to be Autopsied

Pan Ziqing, residing at 55 Seymour Road, loves gambling. His wife, Wang, tried to dissuade him, but he did not change. Sometimes, he even retorted. Wang, feeling extremely resentful, secretly ingested opium paste. The family noticed and sent her to Baolong Hospital. However, the poison had penetrated too deeply, and she could not be revived. She died at the hospital at 7:00 PM on the 4th. Pan took the body back, initially without reporting it to the police station. However, the hospital felt that it was inappropriate to conceal such a death, so it notified the Jing'an Temple police station by telephone. Detectives were dispatched to investigate Pan's home. Because Pan had avoided capture, the body was first taken to the Feilun Road autopsy room. Later, it was learned where Pan was hiding, so he was captured. Yesterday morning, Pan was taken to the autopsy room. Then, Prosecutor Guo of the Special District Local Court arrived at the room for an autopsy. He interrogated Pan, who confessed that the deceased was his wife and that she usually had heart pain. When she had an attack, swallowing soot would relieve the pain slightly. He had been out when she took it this time and did not witness it. Cai Wang, the sister of the deceased, also testified that her sister had not spoken to her before her death, so she did not know the cause of her death. However, soot was found next to the deceased, so it was known that she had taken poison. Prosecutor Guo said that whether Pan Wang's death was caused by poisoning should be determined by the court's forensic doctor and the hospital of the Public Works Department. The case was adjourned to Friday for further hearing. Pan Ziqing was temporarily released on 200 yuan bail.

Theft in Shipping Company Accounting Office 175

Theft and Arrest Together

Tian Zhuoyun, from Shaoxing, worked in the purchasing agent's accounting room downstairs at the Taikoo Shipping Company at No. 22 the Bund, French Concession. The day before yesterday (the 4th), Tian went to the company from his home to work on time. Unexpectedly, as soon as he entered the accounting room, he saw that the door was wide open, the iron chain had been cut, and the drawers on the desk had been opened. The iron door of the safe was wide open. Knowing something was wrong, he checked the miscellaneous items and found that two small silver boxes were missing, containing stocks, real estate deeds, and valuable jewelry, totaling about 15,000 taels. He immediately reported to the purchasing agent and notified the police station. The police chief, hearing the news, immediately led Chinese and Western detectives to rush to the scene for a detailed investigation. They all believed that it was done by someone familiar with the company, not an outside thief. They immediately investigated and found that Jin Hengcan, an employee in the accounting room with Tian, was a major suspect. He was immediately taken to the police station for questioning. Jin confessed the truth, saying that the stolen goods were hidden somewhere in the South City. The police station obtained the confession and immediately recovered the stolen goods. Fortunately, the time had not been long, and there were no losses. He was immediately ordered to be detained.

Arrested for Cashing Forged Treasury Bills 177

Zeng Hai'ao presented fake treasury bills a few days ago to a money house in the French Concession to collect interest. He was discovered by the owner of the money house, who called the police. Zeng was arrested and taken to the police station with the forged treasury bills. He was taken to the French court yesterday for questioning. Punan Corps Police Destroy Bandit Den 178

Rescuing Abductee Zhu Duanzhou

Around 9 PM on the day before yesterday (the 4th), He Baoyi, the head of the Punan (opposite Minhang) Nanhui County Taiping Township Self-Defense Corps, acting on a tip-off, learned that bandits holding an abductee were hiding in Zhuangjiazhai in Dongdu Township, about a li away. Simultaneously, Shao Jingzhi, a patrol officer from the 9th Sub-Bureau of the Zhabei Port Police Station, also received the same information. Thereupon, Head He invited Patrol Officer Shao and summoned Team Leader Pan Chengjiang, Deputy Team Leader He Jianglin, and others from the corps for a secret meeting to discuss countermeasures. Early yesterday morning (the 5th), around 3 AM, Head He personally led Team Leader Pan Chengjiang, Deputy Team Leader He Jianglin, corps members Yan Xiangsheng and Ding Ziliang, along with Gao Liquan, the chief of the 9th Sub-Bureau of Public Security, and Patrol Officer Shao Jingzhi, supervising four capable senior policemen, and proceeded to the location for a quiet search. They first fired a warning shot, then Head He, Team Leaders Pan and He, Chief Gao, Patrol Officer Shao, and Patrol Chief Wang Qikang bravely stormed the bandit den. They rescued abductee Zhu Jizhou on the spot. The bandits fled upon hearing the commotion, and they only captured the bandit's wife, Zhuang Wu, a bandit boat, and seized 20 rounds of ammunition for rapid-fire guns, a gray upper garment uniform, and green woolen jacket and trousers used by the bandits. They brought abductee Zhu Jizhou and others back to the corps headquarters. Under joint interrogation by Head He and Chief Gao, it was revealed that Zhu Jizhou, 57 years old, had been abducted during the bandit raid on Chonggu Town on the 23rd of last month. A sedan chair was hired to send him to the Zhabei Port Public Security Bureau. Subsequently, corps police were dispatched to escort Zhu Jizhou and the bandit's wife, Zhuang Wu, to the Nanhui County Government for further handling.

Natural and Man-Made Disasters in Guangde, Anhui Province 183

Dispatching Personnel to Shanghai to Handle Rice

Guangde, Anhui Province, has suffered from years of drought, and local rice production is no longer sufficient to meet its own needs. Last year, it was hit by natural disasters, with only 30% of the autumn harvest. The price of rice has risen to sixteen or seventeen yuan. The financial situation has further stagnated. Wealthy families have also exported rice in large quantities, depleting supplies. Poor people who relied on odd jobs and loans from wealthy families have no way to seek help, resulting in widespread starvation and rampant banditry. Recently, there were even over a thousand bandits besieging the county seat. Although reinforcements arrived promptly, the city was not captured. However, the people of the county have truly suffered from both natural and man-made disasters. It is said that Wen Jiyu and Wu Xingqing have been dispatched to Shanghai to transport rice for relief.

Special Feature

Xu Peikun's Relief Plan for the Silver Crisis (Continued) 192

(II) Application of the Law of Supply and Demand

Even if we apply the law of supply and demand to this crisis, as some people do, we can still see that some of the opinions expressed at the time were inaccurate. The reduction in the demand for silver is not only less than what some people claim due to the rapid increase in production and the significant decrease in demand, but in fact, production volume has been quite stable in recent years. India's demand for silver has not decreased to an alarming extent, and China's demand for silver has actually increased. A look at the following reliable figures (see Geng Aide's articles on page 6 of the Western Financial Weekly, January 29, 1930, and page 9 of February 6) will prove the above statement to be true.

Table of Shanghai Silver Imports (Average weight of each bar is one tael ounce)

1929: 102,043 (bars)

1928: 112,087

1927: 78,015

1926: 86,310

1925: 65,263

1924: 44,754

1923: 70,882

1922: 39,678

1921: 43,461

1920: 69,136

1919: 47,385

Table of Annual Silver Consumption by Indian Nationals

1929: 92,228,000 standard taels

1928: 70,25,0894

1927: 100,605,870

1926: 129,112,327

1925: 107,892,555

1924: 93,539,360

1923: 100,352,240

1922: 73,104,177

1921: 57,888,119

Since the beginning of 1930, the amount of silver used by China and India has further increased. Based on deductive reasoning, the decline in silver prices should not be so severe and should even rise. As for the price of silver bars, it is indeed set and announced by a few companies in London and New York City. According to the London silver price, the exchange rate parity on the Shanghai event is calculated. As mentioned above, therefore, most people mistakenly believe that the rise and fall of the Shanghai silver exchange rate depends on the fluctuation of the London silver bar price.

(III) Significance of International Exchange Rate Parity Calculation

In the case of gold pounds and silver taels, the most important thing to pay attention to is that when calculating the value of the currency of country B in terms of the currency of country A, the calculation method is to compare the weight of pure gold or pure silver contained in the two currencies. For example, the reason why the pound sterling parity is worth US$4.8665 is only because one US dollar contains 23.22 grams of pure gold, while one British pound contains 111.006 grams of pure gold. However, this kind of parity is by no means the reason for the rise and fall of the pound sterling or US dollar exchange rate. The relationship between Shanghai silver taels and London silver bars is similar to the above. In other words, the relationship between its formula or constant number is a calculation method. Using this method, we calculate the price of Shanghai silver taels with the known London silver price, using shillings and pence. It does not mean that the London silver price determines the Shanghai silver price. The reasons for determining the Shanghai silver price (and the London silver bar price) will be explained in detail below.

(C) The Truth about the Preciousness of Gold and the Cheapness of Silver

Since the occurrence of this problem, the problem is that there is too much empty talk. The most important thing is to understand the real reason for the rise and fall of the silver exchange rate. After understanding the truth, we can go on to seek remedies. Since the problem is complex, scholars must not be swayed by emotions or prejudices. We must deal with it calmly and analyze its state scientifically to gain a full picture of it.

(I) The Beginning of the Financial Crisis: First, let's review the situation when the silver exchange panic first started. The price of standard gold gradually rose last year, and by January 7 of this year, it had risen to a huge amount of 476 taels. At that time, the speculative community, the banking community, the business community, and other related parties showed signs of anxiety, but there was no major disturbance. Until January 8, the price of gold jumped from 476 taels to 496 taels, and then the live drama in the history of gold trading in Shanghai began. After the speculators' failure, they vigorously announced the secrets of standard gold manipulation, and the disturbances against speculation and the maintenance of the silver exchange rate also boiled over. If the price of standard gold had not soared so rapidly at that time (January 8), then the financial disturbances in this port would have been delayed or even indefinitely delayed.

(II) Application of the Principle of International Payment Rule

The key to the problem of standard gold and silver exchange rate is that the silver exchange rate is a reflection of the price of standard gold. The principle of international exchange rate is originally a very difficult and specialized theory, but the state of Shanghai silver exchange rate is even more complicated. According to the simple exchange rate principle, the Shanghai silver exchange rate should change according to the international payment rule, which is the same as the international payment between the two gold-using countries in the ordinary state. However, in the former case, in terms of abstract theory, raw silver is a commodity, and its gold value can also affect the Shanghai silver exchange rate. The application of the international payment rule to this problem is very obvious and does not need to be verified. In short, when our country should pay foreign countries, the silver exchange rate turns against it; conversely, when our country should receive foreign countries, the silver exchange rate turns smoothly. In addition to the smoothness and reversal of international payments as a major reason, there are also more powerful reasons that affect the silver exchange rate, that is, the long-neglected standard gold speculation and the East Exchange.

(III) The Influence of East Exchange on the Silver Exchange Rate: First, please examine the reason for the East Exchange. For several years, the East Exchange has often had a unique hegemonic influence on our country's silver exchange rate due to the relationship of standard gold speculation. Most of the standard gold speculation made for silver exchange rate and the speculation against the silver exchange rate only follow the lead of the East Exchange. When the East Exchange rises, it means that the price of standard gold rises and the silver exchange rate falls; conversely, the same is true. Although the rise and fall of standard gold can also reverberate to the East Exchange, its influence is insignificant compared to the influence of the East Exchange on standard gold. The above-mentioned phenomenon has been going on in China for many years, so our most reasonable conclusion is that the Shanghai silver exchange rate is controlled by the East Exchange, not by the London silver bar price. (To be continued)

Free Talk

A Word or Two Autumn · Water · 193

Modern women, before the age of twenty, have already eaten up the essence of love. So when they reach middle age, they feel that life is dry.

Almost every man can tell you how to marry a woman to be his wife. But no one can explain why he wants to marry her.

Don't judge a woman's nature and appearance by her soft voice on the phone, and don't judge a man's character after he has drunk a glass of iced wine.

Morality used to be a matter of geography, but now it is a matter of time. What was once considered a sin can now be called beautiful. What is now considered terrible may be a very fashionable act in the future.

Women like to recall past love and past dreams, while men like to guess at future happiness and future dreams.

Say this to newlywed friends: "Don't talk too much nonsense. Take more detours. Hurry home." [To people who have been married for a long time: "Wait a moment. There is wine and flowers here. Let's wait for future miracles."

Spring is a soul-stirring weather. Women think, "It would be best to hang the little bell tied around the cat's neck on the husband's lapel."

Gu Tinglin's Shoes - A Record of Politics 194

Gu Tinglin of Kunshan was a man of extensive learning. His book, *Rizhi Lu*, is a great crystallization of our country's scholarship. It has been three hundred years since his death, but his legacy remains, and his great name has not diminished. Yesterday, a friend of mine told me about Mr. Gu's shoes. Although a small matter, it was quite interesting, so I recorded it to enrich this discussion.

The History of the Tomb: Mr. Tinglin's hometown was Qiandun in Kunshan, a place of beautiful scenery. Mr. Gu died in Gan and was never buried in his hometown. His descendants placed his clothes and hat in a coffin and buried him there. During the Xuan Tong reign of the Qing Dynasty, Prince Tutor Liang Dingfen came to Qian to pay respects to the public tomb. He repaired it and built four persimmon pavilions beside the tomb. It is said that Mr. Gu's former residence had four persimmon trees in the courtyard, hence the name was chosen to commemorate him. After the late Qing Dynasty and the Republic of China, there was no one to manage it, and the tomb and ancestral hall fell into disrepair.

The Style of the Shoes: Mr. Gu has a pair of shoes that still exist in his former home. The shoes are over a foot long, with a dull gray surface. The soles are damaged, the opening is quite narrow, and there is a lot of dust on them. Judging from historical speculation, this item is definitely not a common object. It is antique and quite different from ordinary items. Besides this, there is also a red silk shoe of similar size. Both are placed in a glass box.

Legends of the Lost Shoe: The relic is not unusual, but what is strange is that only one shoe remains. According to general rumors, it is said that Mr. Gu, when he died in Gan, specially sent this shoe back to show his descendants. Another theory is that Mr. Gu left it at home in a hurry to go out. The former theory is more credible, but there is no way to verify it. The truth is unknown.

The Origin of the Red Shoes: The red shoes, which are kept in the same container as the lost shoe, are another story entirely.

A Record of Receiving a Ring - He Tianjian 195

This is a record of Sun Xueni giving a ring to Zheng Wuchang. Wuchang is impulsive and irritable. If he disagrees with someone, he will argue. However, once the matter is over, he no longer cares. Wuchang always wants to repent and change, but he cannot. Recently, we had a dinner party at Nanyuan. During the meal, we talked about our views on life. Wuchang spoke highly of the wrongness of his temper. He repented of the past and wanted to warn himself in the future. This is the way of a gentleman. Xueni then took off his ring and gave it to him, saying, "Is it okay to wear this to warn you?" Everyone praised him and said, "Since it is to warn you, it must be done solemnly. How can we act lightly?" They pushed me to be the one to give the ring. I immediately performed the ceremony of giving the ring. Wuchang stood facing Xueni. I stood up and said, "It is admirable for a wise man to know his mistakes and repent. In the past, Ximen Bao wore Wei to restrain himself, so he warned himself against impatience. Now that you have received this ring, there must be an inscription. The inscription says: 'Wei means righteousness.' You should always remember it and examine it with it morning and night." After I finished speaking, I handed it to him with both hands. Wuchang bowed three times and received it. Everyone said, "Many people in this world are self-righteous when they make mistakes. Wuchang is not one of them. How can we not record this? You should write an article to record it." So, I took up my pen and wrote this record.

It is often criticized that the red silk shoe is not similar to the other shoe. However, there is a history to it. When the Nanyang Industrial Exposition was held in Nanjing, relics of ancient sages were collected extensively, including this shoe. Later, the descendants were afraid that this unique souvenir would not survive, so they made a new shoe in the same style to replace it. Later, the shoe was returned and kept with the original. Visitors can see the shoe. As the shoe is a historical souvenir, the Gu family stored it carefully and treasured it greatly. Outsiders can also expand their horizons by visiting with permission.

Anecdotes of the Robbery in Sijing - Cao Wenhai 196

In recent years, bandits have been rampant. Residents in various places are living in anxiety. Even my small town (Sijing, Songyi) was robbed by a large gang of bandits twice last month. The details have been published in local news in various newspapers. Now, I will briefly describe the omissions below.

Disguised as Peddlers: Three or four days before the robbery, the bandits had already mixed into Sijing. They disguised themselves as peddlers selling "silk cotton quilts, foreign thread socks, calico, and children's sweets," etc., shouting in the streets and alleys. Secretly, they scouted the pawnshops and the homes of wealthy people in the town. At about 3 p.m. on the 28th, more than ten bandit ships suddenly arrived and anchored in the west of the town. The bandits landed and formed a team. They first

Fired Shots as a Demonstration: The bandits pre-ambushed as a signal. One bandit at the front carried a large red silk flag with the words "The World's First Army" written on it. They walked from the west market towards the east. At that time, they were spotted by a member of the defense corps on the West Bridge, who fired a shot and killed the flag bearer. The second bandit immediately stepped forward to hold the flag. The member fired another shot, and the second bandit also fell. The third bandit rushed up. The member fired another shot and hit him. Seeing the flag bearers fall one after another, the bandits swarmed to attack the defense corps in an attempt to rob them. Seeing the large group chasing them, the members hurriedly returned to the corps headquarters to report. At that time, the members were building a mud wall at the back door. Upon hearing the report, they each took their weapons and went out through the back door. The bandits had already chased in, and

Both Sides Opened Fire: They fought and retreated to the public sports field near the back of the town. After about an hour and a half of fierce fighting, the members ran out of ammunition, and the bandits who had been pre-ambushed in various places gathered. The situation became more rampant. The members had to retreat temporarily. Seeing that the defense corps was unable to resist, the bandits

Entered the Market to Rob: The robbery lasted about five hours. (The shops robbed and the losses have been detailed in various newspapers, so I will omit them.) At six o'clock, the bandits went to the west of the town to line up and call names. As a result, one person was missing. They re-entered the town and searched with whistles. After searching everywhere, they could not find him. The bandits then

Offered a Large Reward: One bandit held a stack of banknotes and shouted, "Third Brother, Third Master!" He ran wildly in the street. Another bandit cried and said, "If anyone finds Third Master, or finds his body, I am willing to reward 200 yuan." Later, it was increased to 500 yuan, but no one responded. As the weather gradually darkened, the bandits were afraid that the army would catch up and did not dare to linger. They hurriedly fled to the northwest. By the time the Songjiang army arrived in Si, the bandits had already fled far away.

Interesting Anecdotes After the Incident: This month's sixth day was the Catholic pilgrimage to Sheshan by Catholics. Therefore, more and more men and women from all over the world went to Sheshan to visit. One day was a holiday for the World Labor Day Commemoration. More than a dozen of my colleagues took advantage of the holiday to go to Sheshan to play. On the way, we passed through Sijing. We landed at the east market and went to the streets for sightseeing. At that time, the people in the town saw that they did not know more than a dozen people, and their accents were different. So, they started talking. The women who saw it said, "A group of strangers. I don't know what they are doing in Si." It had only been two or three days since the robbery. Seeing strangers, they were already panicked. They were really like startled birds.

This robbery was due to the fact that the authorities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces recently joined forces to encircle and suppress bandits in the Taihu Lake area. The bandits fled east and west, choosing towns and villages without troops to rob. I hope that the magistrates of the various counties will also join forces to encircle and suppress them. If there is a bandit alarm in County A, County B must cooperate to apprehend them upon hearing the report. By joining forces and communicating with each other, the bandits will not succeed and will be easily wiped out. Merchants can also operate with peace of mind. The fact that Sijing was not devastated was all due to the strength of the defense corps. The members were only thirty or forty people, but they were able to fight against more than a hundred bandits. It was really not easy.

A Jealous Wife is a Virtuous Wife - A New Discovery - Li Chubi 197

Lu, a retired gentleman from Shanghai, is a relative of Lu Zhongqi, the former Jiangsu Provincial Treasurer of the Qing Dynasty. He had been an official in Hubei for many years and accumulated a lot of wealth. He is over sixty years old and has two sons and five grandchildren. His wife, Mrs. Yang, is the same age as Lu. Last year, Lu suddenly thought of taking a concubine and discussed it with Mrs. Yang. Mrs. Yang agreed. It is understandable why he would be happy that an old tree would sprout. Lin, a man from Fujian, was living with them. He was an old friend of Lu and is now also a retired gentleman. They both rented a house. Lin is one year younger than Lu. His wife, Mrs. Zhu, is notoriously jealous. Even at banquets, if she finds out that there is a prostitute present, she will question him repeatedly and not allow him to go again. When Lin saw Lu take a concubine, he was very envious. One day, he boldly asked Mrs. Zhu if he could take a concubine, citing Lu's example and saying that the concubine could also serve Mrs. Zhu. Zhu did not allow it, saying, "You are old. Don't you want to live a few more years?" Lin could not get her permission, and the matter ended. Zhu also blamed Yang, saying that she was too muddleheaded. Later, Lu became ill from time to time. He died after only two years. Mrs. Zhu was literate and wrote a eulogy for her husband, which included the line, "Only then do I know that a jealous wife is a virtuous wife." Unfortunately, the narrator could not remember the entire eulogy. At this point, Lin also felt the virtue of Mrs. Zhu and often told people that he was not continuing Lu's legacy because of his wife. He said, "I am fortunate that my wife is unwilling to adopt an open policy." When I heard this, I said, "In the past, Emperor Wen of Sui always resented Empress Dugu's jealousy. Only after Empress Dugu died did the emperor dare to indulge himself in the concubines. Before long, his body failed. He lamented, 'If Empress Dugu were still alive, I would not be like this.' Although the emperor knew he was wrong, it was too late." I also heard that Yu Hong of Suzhou, a *juren* of the Guangxu Jiawu year, had no sons. After taking a concubine and having a son, his wife did not allow him to enter the concubine's room. She was also approaching sixty years of age at that time. After his wife died, there was no one to restrain him. He died not long after. Looking at this, a jealous wife is indeed a virtuous wife because she can protect her husband's health. However, for thousands of years, they have been unjustly accused of jealousy. How unjust!

Another Column

Presented to Magistrate Xu Wenbin of Zhuji - Yu Chongyao 198

The two Xu magistrates in our county are admired like an old couple. After sixty years of calamity, the dangerous city has been rebuilt. During the Xian Tong years of the Qing Dynasty, the Yue rebellion was raging. Magistrate Xu of Xiangxi (Magistrate Xu Xuemen Yaoguang) stood firm and defended the city. He repelled the Yellow Turbans. After the war, he resumed his duties and brought a withered county back to life. Even today, old men with white hair can still talk about it with tears in their eyes. Last year, war broke out again. The Qian Ge armies were again rampant. Zhejiang was suffering from frequent military communications and troop movement. The army was pressing on the west, and the quake was coming from the east. Zhuyang was at a strategic crossroads. Magistrate Xu of Wumen foresaw the danger and consulted the gentleman Wei Shen. He made an early plan to cut off the flue to prevent fire. The war became increasingly chaotic, and troops were stationed everywhere. Hundreds of thousands of soldiers from Zhu Ti were conscripted, and millions of bundles of hay were requisitioned. Everything was forcibly demanded, and the robbery continued until the end of winter. The land was crisscrossed by boundaries, and the corners of the chairs were used as landmarks in the conflicts. The Nine Passes were guarded by tigers and leopards, and the wilderness was occupied by foxes and rabbits. Roaming riders acted like Zhuang Qiao. They broke through walls and robbed roofs, searching chests and emptying cotton-padded jackets. Food was reduced to feed the soldiers, and even rough rice was not enough to eat. The generals' mansions were deep, and their ears were deaf to the cries of the people. Thousands of villages were evacuated, and people carried their families and infants. They trudged through ice and cold rain. They were lost in the fields, pushing and shoving each other in the mud. The villages were deserted, and the wind and dust obscured the view. In the bleak rain and snow, there was no dawn for hundreds of miles. Magistrate Xu said, "Do not be afraid. I will protect your safety." He was not afraid of their intimidating power and stood firm. In his calmness, he never wavered. In the midst of danger, how much humiliation did he endure? I live in the south of the city and gaze at the situation. I call him General Bo and cling to him like Liu Biao. On New Year's Eve, we stood together, surrounded by swords and spears. We dared to provoke the Asura's wrath, and a mutiny was only seconds away. We celebrated our survival, and the spring scenery was clear. Looking back on the aftermath of the pain, I feel a hundred emotions in my heart. We formed a pact and became friends like Guan Bao. In Chang'an, the game of chess is being played, and the actions are all chaotic. The jade is half-cut and sold for wine, and Yangcheng should be examined. You then hung up your documents and returned home, following the Zhushui and the Hongniao. People lined the roads to welcome you, old and young. We offer our heartfelt wishes to Zhu of Tongxiang and Zhao of the embroidered plain. The Goucheng is luxuriant, and the Huanjiang flows vast. The mountains are high and the waters are long, all praised by the Jiazao. The two Xu magistrates in our county are not praying for private blessings. Thousands of mouths will carve a monument to your achievements. We should cherish this fame as treasure. Also ask, sincerely seek. There are no other tricks. The upright officials are from Han Xijing. Who can compare to you without you? Fear the fortresses and celebrate Geng Sang, Xie Tiao of Qingshan. I will write this poem on New Year's Eve, and also record my lifelong friendship.

Eastern Travel Correspondence (5) - Wu Xiaohou 199

(5) Inspection of Tokyo

(A) Municipal Administration: Japan calls Tokyo, Yokohama, Nagoya, Kyoto, Osaka, and Kobe the six major cities. Broadly speaking, Tokyo is a political district, Yokohama, Osaka, and Kobe are industrial and commercial districts, Nagoya (also known as Chukyo, the first capital of Japan) and Kyoto (also known as Kyoto, the former capital of Japan) are scenic districts. The municipal administration of these six major cities has made significant progress based on the relationship between region and personnel, and there is a constant eagerness for improvement. Tokyo, in particular, is the capital of Japan. After the great earthquake, the Japanese government established a Reconstruction Bureau under the Ministry of Interior to plan and implement national reconstruction projects. It also established a Tokyo Municipal Reconstruction Bureau to reconstruct the capital. It is making every effort to do so. When the reporter arrived in Tokyo, it was just as the city's reconstruction project had been successfully completed, and the Reconstruction Bureau was about to be abolished. The precision of its planning and the grandeur of its construction are vastly different from the progress before the earthquake. Therefore, carrying a letter of introduction from the Japanese Ministry of Interior, accompanied by Mr. Uchida Takeo, an interpreter from the Japan-China Association, and Miss Du Huairong, with a camera, I first went to the Tokyo City Hall (i.e., the City Hall) to visit and investigate. It happened that the city's Mayor, Mr. Hori Kiri Zenjiro, was visiting Kyoto for the Grand Shrine of Ise Grand Ceremony. (Kyoto is the former capital, so the Japanese government stipulates that all of the country's emperor's enthronement ceremonies and the Grand Thanksgiving Festival, i.e., the Grand Sacrifice Ceremony, are permanently held here. The ceremony is extremely grand.) The Chief Deputy Mayor, Mr. Shirakami Yūkichi, and Secretary Tanigawa Noboru, came out to meet us. The reporter inquired about the situation of Tokyo's municipal administration. According to the response, Tokyo is the capital of the country and has a special situation. There are many issues to be addressed. Now, I will list the circumstances of the answers to the questions and the facts of the personal visit in detail below. (1) Overview of the Organization of the Tokyo City Hall: Because of its status as the capital, the Tokyo City Hall has three assistant mayors under the mayor. (The assistant mayor is the deputy mayor.) Other cities have two assistant mayors. In addition to assisting the mayor, the assistant mayor is in charge of the bureaus and departments of the city hall. (A) First Assistant Mayor Shirakami Yūkichi is in charge of the Finance Bureau, the Electricity Bureau, the Accounting Division, the Audit Division, the Commerce and Industry Division, the Electricity Research Institute, etc. (1) The Finance Bureau has four divisions: Accounting, Revenue, Management, and Geography. The director of the bureau is concurrently held by the assistant mayor. (2) The Electricity Bureau has eleven divisions: General Affairs, Labor, Management, Accounting, Transportation, Electric Lights, Electricity, Engineering, Vehicles, the Automotive Division, and the High-Speed Railway Investigation Division, as well as factories and the Electric Bureau Hospital. The director of the bureau is Mr. Mizo Masataro. (3) The Accounting Division has four sections: General Affairs, Payment, Revenue, and Recording. (A section is like a share in our country. One section is one share.) (4) The Audit Division has three sections: General Affairs, Audit, and Inspection. (5) The Commerce and Industry Division has seven sections: General Affairs, Industry, Finance, Slaughterhouse, the Central Market, the Retail Market, and Weights and Measures, as well as the Green Fruit Market and the Fish Market. (6) The Electricity Research Institute has three divisions: First, Second, and Third. (2) Second Assistant Mayor Tanaka Kotaro is in charge of the Social Bureau, the Education Bureau, the Health Bureau, the Nursery Home, the Secretariat, and the Documents Division, etc. (1) The Social Bureau has three divisions: Public Operation, Protection, and Employment, as well as the Neighborhood Welfare Center, the Work Training Center, and the Employment Agency. The director of the bureau is Mr. Yasui Seiichiro. (2) The Education Bureau has three divisions: School Affairs, Supervision, and Social Education, as well as the Teacher Training Institute and the Library. The director of the bureau is Mr. Fujii Toshitaka. (3) The Health Bureau has three divisions: Hygiene, Sanitation, and Parks, as well as the Hygiene Experiment Institute. The director of the bureau is concurrently held by the director of the Social Bureau. (4) The Nursery Home has four divisions: General Affairs, Guardianship, Medical Labor, and Management, as well as the Sugamo Branch, the Itabashi Branch, the Awa Branch, and the Inogashira School. The director of the home is Mr. Shibusawa Eiichi. (5) The Secretariat has one secretary-general and two secretaries. (6) The Documents Division has six sections: Documents, General Affairs, Regulations, Investigation, Correspondence, and Labor. (3) Third Assistant Mayor Hirose Hisanaka is in charge of the Water Bureau, the Civil Engineering Bureau, and the Reconstruction Bureau, etc. (1) The Water Bureau has six divisions: Water Supply, Water Purification, General Affairs, River Ports, Sewage, and Construction, as well as the Wharf Office. The director of the bureau is Mr. Konda Shinzaburo. (3) The Reconstruction Bureau has three divisions: Facility Construction, Construction Work, and General Affairs, as well as the First, Second, Third, and Fourth Branch Offices. The director of the bureau is Mr. Fukuda Shigeyoshi. The above bureaus and divisions, except for the Reconstruction Bureau, are all permanent institutions. There are also fifteen ward offices under the City Hall (like the current district offices in our country). The ward chiefs, under the direction of the mayor, are responsible for managing the affairs of their respective wards. The organization, evolution, and current situation of the ward system will be discussed in a separate article.

Gold Market Soars 202

Up 2.9 taels

The gold price rebounded yesterday, with only half a day of trading in the morning session. The premium rose to a high point, fluctuating around 3 taels. The foreign exchange rate initially eased but then tightened. HSBC's quoted rate was long in the morning but then shortened. Demand exceeded supply among dealers, and the market was bullish. Zihfeng Yong, Dadecheng, and Yuancheng Yong were keen to buy, while Shunli, Wanxing, and Yuanmaoyong were selling short positions. The large bars were also long in the morning, so they fell slightly, then hovered around 504 taels. The difference was almost one tael. Later, both official and unofficial foreign exchange bills were bullish. The near-term Japanese gold was calculated at 1.06375, and the British gold was only 0.109375. By noon, the trend was gradually upward, reaching 507 taels. Buyers became more active, and British silver bars rose by 1/16, while silver prices also increased by 1/4. The exchange rate was as before. At the beginning, the trend was slightly lower, hovering around the June premium opening at 504.1 taels, slightly down 0.02 taels. However, the gross price suddenly fell, fluctuating by about 1 tael. Wanxing, Shunli, and Dadecheng all entered, while Yucheng Yong and retail investors exited. The price fell from 4.5-4.6 to 3.6-3.7 taels. The first announcement was around 4 taels, but the quoted price was already up 0.0125, the US dollar was up 0.0025, and the Japanese gold was down 0.000625. The internal market remained flat and was not affected. Zhengjin absorbed the June Japanese gold at 1.055. Sumitomo and Huabi and Xingye traded June British gold at 0.1125. HSBC then bought the current month at the same price, and the gold price fluctuated around 5 taels.
