Silk and Tea: Spring Races Make the Silk Market Quiet

Yesterday was the second day of the Spring Races in Shanghai. Foreign firms followed their usual practice of closing early in the afternoon for the holiday. Silk merchants only had half a day of business in the morning. Overseas silk sales were stagnant, and there were no telegrams from overseas regarding silk. European and American firms were passive. Senior staff members were away on vacation, further depressing the silk market. There were no reported transactions.

Scarce Leases for Xiaoshao Cocoon Firms 208

This year, due to unrest in Xiaoshan and Shaoxing, farmers reduced the number of silkworms they raised. Only households near the city and towns continued to raise silkworms. The silkworms are currently feeding on the best mulberry leaves. Improved silkworm breeds have not been significantly affected, but native breeds have been largely abandoned due to unfavorable weather conditions. There are few silkworms, but ample leaves. Mulberry leaf prices are generally only 1.50 or 1.60 yuan. In previous years, cocoon firms in the area would have already been fully leased. Staff would have arrived with funds to prepare for the opening of cocoon buying. This year, due to ongoing banditry, silk and cocoon merchants are hesitant. Few cocoon firms have been leased. Statistics show that less than 10-20% of the cocoon firms in Xiaoshan and Shaoxing have been leased. The reduced activity in the cocoon market this year is distressing.

Qifu Red Tea Stalled 209

Since the Qifu new red tea gardens opened in recent days, tea production has been slow and often suspended due to cloudy and rainy weather, which increases the time required for farmers to harvest and process tea. Yesterday, new tea from the Fulu area was opening at a price of 60 yuan per dan, while Qilu tea was higher, at 12 yuan, similar to last year. However, most of the major tea companies that typically fix prices at the river ports have not yet gone into the mountains, making it difficult to open the market. As a result, while prices for new tea from mountain farmers and upper estates can be lowered, tea companies cannot afford to take the risk. The Qifu tea market is virtually stalled.

After Opening New Tea Sales, British Companies Suddenly Hesitate 210

Yesterday, the local Shanghai foreign-owned tea market and tea factories exhibited a small amount of new samples of precious eyebrow green tea at tea warehouses. British company experts began to hesitate. Besides the precious eyebrow tea sale agreed upon the other day, there were no other business openings.

Dexing New Tea Heard to be Weighed 211

This year's Dexing new green tea was harvested early because of earlier weather and quiet bandit areas. In the past two days, the new tea in the area of ​​Xinjiang, Huangjiajian, Shanling and Suyao has been collected in small amounts by tea vendors, and sold at a price of five corners per catty. Mountain farmers sell as soon as they collect and do not store it at all. Although the price is low, they are willing to sell first (April 29).

Tunxi New Tea News 212

Tunxi tea market has become increasingly lively in recent days. There have been more than 60 tea houses and companies that have organized openings. The mountain farmers are currently busy with harvesting, and the harvest will not be very low. However, because Tunxi City suffered from bandit disasters last year, and tea merchants also suffered losses, the vitality of the city was severely damaged. In addition, Shanghai tea warehouses are extremely strict with releasing money to Tunxi, resulting in tight money and difficult operations. Currently, only Dafang Garden Tea in various new tea markets in Tunxi has opened for 80 yuan per dan. Other prices have not yet been determined.

Food: Rice Market on the Lower River Varies in Strength 213

Medium and Secondary Rice Continues to be Generally Weak

Yesterday, few rice boats from the interior arrived in Zhabei. However, there were active stockpiles on the Lower River, so market sales still did not improve. Due to thin supply and sales of North Gang's top grade white japonica rice at both production and sales sites, cargo owners are reluctant to lower prices due to cost considerations. However, medium and secondary grade japonica rice stocks are large, and sales are sluggish. Only the newly arrived top and medium grade japonica rice are slightly active, while other transactions are light, leading to price reductions. Thin paddy rice arrivals were weak, demand was dull, and the trend continues to be weak. However, the true top grade goods must be outside the 19 yuan customs. Yangxian is stable. Dujian rice follows the movement of foreign rice. Because the flow of scarce goods is rare, buyers do not pay much attention. There are few changes in the overall market. White yuan rice is in high demand, while lower grades are stagnant, indicating a tendency to raise the price of higher grades and suppress the price of lower grades. Overall trading volume was extremely light.

More than a dozen boats arrived at Hunan Inner Road. The buying interest on this street was extremely quiet. Only the Chang Gang high-quality rice was stable. The sales of common japonica rice from Xibang were slow. However, the market price can still be maintained. Sutong machinery japonica rice is mostly numb. Because of few high-quality and many low-quality rices, customers are unwelcome. There will have to be a difference of one corner on the rise and fall of the market price. On the surface, it still seems flat. Buyers of South Gang's thin early paddy rice are generally watching because they do not want to stockpile it at this time of year. Foreign rice is also suppressing the local market, which is especially not enjoyable. The market situation is the most sluggish. Foreign Duji and other points, except for South Gang, have also arrived sporadically in Tongli and other places. Since customers have foreign rice in hand, their desire to consume local rice is poor, and the overall market feels dull and soft. Changes are subtle and the situation is very weak. Transactions are scarce and the price for high-quality rice is strong, while the price for lower grades is weak.

The Key to the Flour Market Remains in the Weather 214

Predicted Wheat Harvest to be Above 80%

Yesterday, the flour market showed a flat and weak trend. Although North's sales of flour will be good this month, manufacturers such as Fufeng and Fuxin do not have consistent attitudes, so even though the trend is good, some people remain hesitant. As for the long-term futures, the weather is sunny, and the climate is favorable, so market sentiment has softened. According to industry insiders, if this type of weather does not change within half a month, then this year's wheat harvest should be above 80%, an increase of 20% compared to previous years. Therefore, the key to this year's new wheat harvest will depend on the situation within the month. As a result, this month's price was slightly smaller than the previous day's by five li. Each of the months of June, July and August were lower by one fen. The September was smaller by one fen and two li, and the October was also lower by seven li.

Large-Scale Activity by Short Sellers in the Wheat Market 215

It is Difficult for Xibang Bulls to Maintain Their Position

Yesterday, the price of wheat futures fell sharply across the board. Foreign wheat was reported to be lower by one or two jiao, and the weather was very good. The situation, which had previously seemed to favor maintaining the position, has been influenced by the weather. The rain on the ground is related to the abundance or lack of wheat, and the possibility of the price of this new wheat falling exists. Therefore, in both the morning and afternoon sessions, the selling of new short sellers was intense. Those who wanted to maintain a firm bullish position were only from Xibang. However, the environment was unfavorable, and the prices were slightly lower. As a result, the price of wheat for June fell by four cents compared to the previous day, July by two cents, August by two cents, and September and October by three cents. Spot wheat remained flat, as sales and deliveries were evenly matched, and there was little fluctuation. Anqing and Hankou wheat was sold for 4.32 to 4.07 taels.

It also includes inscriptions from Hu Shih and Hsu Shih-ying. Important works such as "Cash Fraud," "What is the Purpose of Accounting," and "Explanation of the Principles of Debit and Credit" are included, which can express what others cannot in the field of accounting. The company has decided to enlarge and change the format to a sixteenmo size starting from the sixth issue and increase the price. Subscriptions starting from the first issue will remain unchanged.

Automobile News

Special Article

Small Contributions to Increase Business by Cheng Zhizheng 225

When a salesperson has two or three hundred clients, there are two ways to look at it. It can be seen as a tedious chore, or it can be seen as a gold mine. If the gold mine is mined properly, there will naturally be good returns. Otherwise, the result will certainly not be good. For example, if there are three hundred customers, there are three hundred cars that need to be serviced every month, whether it's lubrication, washing, or tire and battery replacement. The work is very intense.

Among the three hundred clients, some tend to forget the service period. Therefore, salespeople should think of ways to notify them and attract their attention. Success or failure hinges on this. From an economic point of view, there are several new scientific methods worth introducing for agile service.

(1) Reminder slips are the latest style, and they are already being used in many places. The method is to stick a printed slip on the car's speedometer, which clearly states the various requirements, such as how many miles to drive before refueling, how many days to wash, and other common knowledge. In this way, the car owner can be alerted at any time when turning off the car and will not forget. The price of this kind of reminder slip is very low, and the beauty lies in this point, and the function is great. However, many car owners do not like to stick paper on the car, but now the reminder slips are printed very beautifully, and the car owner can use them as a kind of decoration. If they really don't want to, they can stick them underneath.

Postcards are the second inexpensive method. When the repair period for a certain customer arrives, you can notify them with a postcard. When he sees the postcard, he will of course come. Some people advocate that salespeople print a special kind of postcard, which must be special, otherwise it will be unclear.

On the contrary, it is not good. This is indeed true. It is best to print some colored ones, which will be more meaningful. Now there are also machines used to manage photos automatically. For example, if a certain customer needs to repair on that day, make a mark on that day, and when that day arrives, it will naturally fall down, and you can mail it immediately without forgetting. (3) Letters Letters are more expensive than postcards. The printing paper costs two cents per letter, and three hundred letters per month cost six yuan. Adding postage is even more alarming. However, letters also have one advantage, which is that they are more formal than postcards and are easily valued. The effect is also great. Although the price is high, judging from the harvest, writing letters is also worthwhile.

(4) Telephone The telephone is another step further. Direct communication with the customer is more direct than writing a letter. When a person receives a letter, he can stuff it in his pocket or even discard it. Perhaps after reading it, he forgets it due to being busy. This is a common occurrence. Now that you can talk to him directly, he will naturally pay special attention, and the degree of forgetting will naturally be much less. Moreover, customers with telephones are relatively richer and can take advantage of this to do other transactions. However, the only difficulty with telephones is that the cost is too high. Some telephone bills are calculated monthly, and some are calculated by the number of times. If calculated by the number of times, the burden is even heavier. However, if the effect is great, this small fee is naturally not a problem. Telephones can not only increase trade, but also assist in the shortcomings of postcards. If you do not receive it or forget to receive it, you can urge it by telephone. The two impressions are deeper and will never be forgotten again. Telephone calls are also very cost-effective when business is slow. If calculated monthly, business is naturally not a problem when busy. Now, don’t ask if the telephone is expensive or not, just ask if the work is efficient. If the efficiency is checked, the telephone bill is not a problem.

In short, after a salesperson sells a car, he must also pay attention to service. To provide service, you must always pay attention to the customer's period of need. When the period arrives, you must notify him. First, maintain your own business and avoid being snatched by others. Second, it is also a kind of goodwill towards the customer. To maintain this kind of business, the four methods mentioned above are all new and desirable. Because it is more difficult for customers to come to the door themselves, use reminders to make customers pay attention to themselves, and use postcards, letters, and telephones to urge customers to pay attention. Therefore, the former is automatic, and the latter is passive. The last is to advance on both sides, then the effect will be more significant. Finally, I can say that things are done by people. When he is a gold mine, he can naturally profit. When he is an annoyance, failure is undoubtedly. In addition to the above methods, a person must also have patience and perseverance. If he can do this, success is not a problem.

Fisk Tires that Turn Danger into Safety 226

Rough and arduous journeys are no different from flat ground

Recently, two Peruvians and two Chileans made a car trip. All that has been passed through has been unprecedented. They set off from Santiago, Chile on the morning of September 16. They lived in a Packard car equipped with Fisk tires. They opened mountains and made roads. Giant rocks and boulders were everywhere. The view was desolate. It was a barren land.

What is called a road is actually a tooth-like rock. The tire goes through it, and the disaster is unavoidable. When the tire was manufactured, it did not initially undergo this kind of test to determine its needs. After this amazing test, Fisk wheels have further proved that their tires are manufactured with experience that matches the name. The slope of the car’s path ranges from 40 degrees to 50 degrees, and the ascent from the horizontal line varies up to 7,000 feet. As for the height of the caves and the strangeness of the rocks, they are all on the way, not included in the calculation. Once, the car they were driving suddenly got stuck in a mud pit. Later, it was pulled out of danger by two ox carts. Another time, because the crane could not bear the weight of the entire car Above is a group photo of Mr. Freeman, manager of the China Automobile Company, and Mr. Zhou Mengxian, Chinese manager. Mr. Zhou is young and knowledgeable, quick to act, kind in nature, and widely traveled. All the important figures in the political and business circles are happy to associate with Zhou. He has been serving the company for thirteen years. The company's business can be flourishing, and Mr. Zhou and others have manpower.

Instead of walking, they passed through the center of the Andes Mountains and reached the city of Lima, Peru on October 17. This trip's adventures and unexpected encounters are truly beyond everything. The endurance of human beings belongs to the passengers, the endurance of the car belongs to the machinery, and the durability of the material belongs to the tires.

It is obvious and undoubted.

The entire journey was rugged and uneven, almost impossible to walk an inch. There are deep valleys, mountain peaks, and cliffs. The deepest ones are about 10,000 feet. The climate is also extremely different, ranging from freezing point to 100 degrees Fahrenheit. However, the group of four was able to escape the danger. It can also be said to be dangerous. Anyone who slightly imagines the dangers that these digital drivers have passed through will be amazed. Most of the roads traveled have been measured. Falling onto a barge, when it fell from above, the front right wheel of the car was hitting the side of the barge. The entire weight of the car was pressing on the wheel, but the tire did not burst. The result was that the car body overturned.

The most difficult part of the entire journey was the section through the Atacama Desert. This desert is no different from the Sahara of South America. In the 700-kilometer journey, the water source was cut off. If there is any mistake in human beings or machinery, there is no way to call for help. They passed through this hot sandy land as if in a natural furnace. The terrible hot sun made people thirsty and hot. completely despair. If the car is damaged or the tires are broken, the danger to life is inevitable.

All the difficulties mentioned above and others can be expressed.

Page 28

. I know that in countries around the world, there are several machines every day. Devote your heart and soul to solving various obstacles in car driving. Today, all beings in the world can cross barren and dangerous places as if walking on a flat avenue, with the convenience of safety and comfort. Today's construction should meet the needs of the future.

Shanghai-Taicang Increases Passenger Bus Services by Fan 227

The Shanghai-Taicang long-distance bus route starts from Datong Road in Zhabei, Shanghai, and ends at Liuhe Town in Taicang County, passing through Dachang, Luodian, and Liuhang. It is more than seventy Chinese miles long. It has been in operation for ten years. In the beginning, there were few passengers and sluggish business, and it almost stopped several times. Fortunately, the founders of the company worked hard to maintain it and managed it diligently. After years of painstaking planning, today's good results have been achieved. Today's road is also a model for long-distance buses in various provinces.

This spring, after the completion of the Shanghai-Jiading branch line, business developed even more. Recently, the company has been striving for progress in the application of shares on the entire road in order to win the hearts of passengers. The road base has been solidified, and the road surface is repaired from time to time. It is smooth and flat. The car runs on it without any tilting. The vehicles have also been improved. The old and dilapidated vehicles have been completely eliminated and replaced with new ones. The trees along the way are lush and lush, and the scenery is quite good. Passengers do not feel the bitterness of the journey.

The road has become increasingly crowded with passengers. The station is full. When the passenger bus departs, several vehicles are connected, and there is no empty seat. In view of the large number of passengers, the company increased the number of passenger buses starting from May 1 for convenience. The newly revised timetable is published on the left for reference.

Miscellany

The Question of Passenger Safety on Buses by Zhuo 229

Not long ago, Shanghai newspapers reported on a bus overturning on Jiangwan Road, crushing a ticket seller to death and injuring passengers. This means that the safety of bus passengers is worth discussing and consulting. To ensure the safety of passengers, drivers should first be properly trained. Inexperienced drivers are prone to accidents. This can be seen from the recent case of a certain gentleman running over a certain doctor. However, the responsibility for the misfortune of a bus overturning cannot be placed solely on the driver. Why? Please briefly discuss it.

The quality of the bus's construction has a great impact on the safety of the bus's operation. According to Percival White, an American automotive industry expert, the center of gravity of the bus is related to the overturning of the bus. Most people think that double-decker buses are easier to overturn than single-decker buses. This is not entirely the case. Whether the bus is single-decker or double-decker, its speed should not exceed the maximum limit. Otherwise, the center of gravity of the bus cannot be reduced, and the misfortune of overturning occurs. According to Mr. White, the bus's engine must be flexible. The brake is the convenient way to stop the bus. Many buses, especially public buses, often have various internal mechanisms that are not very flexible due to insufficient consideration of the price. I once asked on the Yuhang bus road. There have been many times when the bus overturned. The reason is that it could not be arbitrarily braked when encountering turns. And the reason why it cannot be arbitrarily braked is mostly because the brake is not flexible. Mr. White said that the failure of the bus to overturn is due to the fact that the arc line cannot be shortened when . This is also related to the road and is not solely the responsibility of the bus's construction.

Also, bus overturning accidents occur more often with buses that solicit passengers (commonly known as "wild chicken buses"). This is because their buses are mostly old and dilapidated. Perhaps, cracking down on old and dilapidated buses is also an item that should be paid attention to by the municipal government.
